  83 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick upper;

  85 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState pool1;
  86 |     |     }

  88 |     |     modifier tickPreconditions(int24 lower, int24 upper) {
  89 | *r  |         require(lower < upper);
  90 | *r  |         require(upper < 887272);
  91 | *r  |         require(lower > -887272);
  92 | *r  |         require(lower % tickSpacing == 0);
  93 | *r  |         require(upper % tickSpacing == 0);
  94 |     |         _;
  95 |     |     }
  96 |     | 
  97 |     |     constructor() {
  98 |     |         manager = new LimitPoolManager();
  99 |     |         factory = new LimitPoolFactory(address(manager));
 100 |     |         implementation = address(new LimitPool(address(factory)));
 101 |     |         rangePool = new PositionERC1155(address(factory));
 102 |     |         
 103 |     |         manager.enableImplementation(bytes32(0x0), address(implementation), address(rangePool));
 104 |     |         tickSpacing = 10;
 105 |     |         tokenIn = new Token20("IN", "IN", 18);
 106 |     |         tokenOut = new Token20("OUT", "OUT", 18);
 107 |     |         (address poolAddr,) = factory.createLimitPool(bytes32(0x0), address(tokenIn), address(tokenOut), 500, 79228162514264337593543950336);
 108 |     |         pool = LimitPool(poolAddr);
 109 |     |     }

 111 | *   |     function mint(uint128 amount, bool zeroForOne, int24 lower, int24 upper) public tickPreconditions(lower, upper) {
 112 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
 113 | *   |         mintAndApprove();
 114 | *   |         amount = amount + 1;
 115 |     |         // Ensure the newly created position is using different ticks
 116 | *   |         for(uint i = 0; i < positions.length;) {
 117 |     |             if(positions[i].owner == msg.sender && positions[i].lower == lower && positions[i].upper == upper && positions[i].zeroForOne == zeroForOne) {
 118 |     |                 revert("Position already exists");
 119 |     |             }
 120 |     |             unchecked {
 121 |     |                 ++i;
 122 |     |             }
 123 |     |         }
 124 |     | 
 125 | *   |         PoolValues memory poolValues;
 126 | *   |         PoolStructs memory poolStructs;
 127 | *   |         LiquidityDeltaValues memory values;
 128 |     | 
 129 | *   |         (,poolStructs.pool0, poolStructs.pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore,poolValues.positionIdNextBefore,,) = pool.globalState();
 130 | *   |         poolValues.price0Before = poolStructs.pool0.price;
 131 | *   |         poolValues.liquidity0Before = poolStructs.pool0.liquidity;
 132 | *   |         poolValues.price1Before = poolStructs.pool1.price;
 133 | *   |         poolValues.liquidity1Before = poolStructs.pool1.liquidity;
 134 |     | 
 135 | *   |         (, poolStructs.lower) = pool.ticks(lower);
 136 | *   |         (, poolStructs.upper) = pool.ticks(upper);
 137 |     | 
 138 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
 139 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
 140 |     | 
 141 | *   |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params;
 142 | *   |         params.to = msg.sender;
 143 | *   |         params.amount = amount;
 144 | *   |         params.mintPercent = 0;
 145 | *   |         params.lower = lower;
 146 | *   |         params.upper = upper;
 147 | *   |         params.zeroForOne = zeroForOne;
 148 |     | 
 149 |     |         // Get the ticks the position will be minted with rather than what was passed directly by fuzzer
 150 |     |         // This is so the we can properly compare before and after mint states of particular ticks.
 151 | *   |         bool posCreated;
 152 | *   |         (lower, upper, posCreated) = pool.getResizedTicksForMint(params);
 153 | *   |         emit PositionTicks(lower, upper);
 154 | *   |         emit PositionCreated(posCreated);
 155 |     | 
 156 |     |         // ACTION 
 157 | *r  |         pool.mintLimit(params);
 158 |     |         if (posCreated) positions.push(Position(msg.sender, poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, lower, upper, zeroForOne));
 159 |     | 
 160 |     |         (, poolStructs.lower) = pool.ticks(lower);
 161 |     |         (, poolStructs.upper) = pool.ticks(upper);
 162 |     | 
 163 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
 164 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
 165 |     | 
 166 |     |         values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter = poolStructs.lower.liquidityDelta;
 167 |     |         values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter = poolStructs.upper.liquidityDelta;
 168 |     | 
 169 |     |         (, poolStructs.pool0, poolStructs.pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter,,,) = pool.globalState();
 170 |     |         poolValues.price0After = poolStructs.pool0.price;
 171 |     |         poolValues.liquidity0After = poolStructs.pool0.liquidity;
 172 |     |         poolValues.price1After = poolStructs.pool1.price;
 173 |     |         poolValues.liquidity1After = poolStructs.pool1.liquidity;
 174 |     |         poolValues.price0 = poolStructs.pool0.price;
 175 |     |         poolValues.price1 = poolStructs.pool1.price;
 176 |     |         
 177 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
 178 |     |         emit Prices(poolValues.price0, poolValues.price1);
 179 |     |         assert(poolValues.price0 >= poolValues.price1);
 180 |     |         // Ensure prices have not crossed
 181 |     |         emit Prices(poolValues.price0After, poolValues.price1After);
 182 |     |         assert(poolValues.price0After >= poolValues.price1After);
 183 |     | 
 184 |     |         // Ensure liquidityDelta is always less or equal to liquidityAbsolute
 185 |     |         emit LiquidityDeltaAndAbsolute(values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
 186 |     |         assert(int256(values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter) <= int256(uint256(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter)));
 187 |     |         emit LiquidityDeltaAndAbsolute(values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
 188 |     |         assert(int256(values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter) <= int256(uint256(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter)));
 189 |     |         
 190 |     |         // Ensure that liquidityAbsolute is incremented when not undercutting
 191 |     |         if(zeroForOne){
 192 |     |             if(poolValues.price0After >= poolValues.price0Before){
 193 |     |                 emit LiquidityAbsolute(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
 194 |     |                 assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter >= poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore);
 195 |     |             }
 196 |     |         } else {
 197 |     |             if(poolValues.price1Before >= poolValues.price1After){
 198 |     |                 emit LiquidityAbsolute(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
 199 |     |                 assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter >= poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore);
 200 |     |             }
 201 |     |         }
 202 |     | 
 203 |     |         if (posCreated) {
 204 |     |             emit PositionTicks(lower, upper);
 205 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed
 206 |     |             assert(lower < upper);
 207 |     |             // Ensure minted ticks on proper tick spacing
 208 |     |             assert((lower % tickSpacing == 0) && (upper % tickSpacing == 0));
 209 |     |         }
 210 |     |         
 211 |     |         emit LiquidityGlobal(poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter);
 212 |     |         emit Liquidity(poolValues.liquidity0Before, poolValues.liquidity1Before, poolValues.liquidity0After, poolValues.liquidity1After);
 213 |     |         
 214 |     |         // Ensure liquidityGlobal is incremented after mint
 215 |     |         assert(poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter >= poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore);
 216 |     |         
 217 |     |         // Ensure pool liquidity is non-zero after mint with no undercuts
 218 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 219 |     |             if (poolValues.price0After < poolValues.price0Before) assert(poolValues.liquidity0After > 0);
 220 |     |         }
 221 |     |         else {
 222 |     |             if (poolValues.price1After > poolValues.price1Before) assert(poolValues.liquidity1After > 0);
 223 |     |         }
 224 |     |     }

 342 | *   |     function swap(uint160 priceLimit, uint128 amount, bool exactIn, bool zeroForOne) public {
 343 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
 344 | *   |         mintAndApprove();
 345 |     | 
 346 | *   |         LimitPoolStructs.SwapParams memory params;
 347 | *   |         params.to = msg.sender;
 348 | *   |         params.priceLimit = priceLimit;
 349 | *   |         params.amount = amount;
 350 | *   |         params.exactIn = exactIn;
 351 | *   |         params.zeroForOne = zeroForOne;
 352 | *   |         params.callbackData = abi.encodePacked(address(this));
 353 |     |         
 354 |     |         // ACTION
 355 | *r  |         pool.swap(params);
 356 |     | 
 357 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
 358 |     |         (,PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool0, PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool1,,,,) = pool.globalState();
 359 |     |         uint160 price0 = pool0.price;
 360 |     |         uint160 price1 = pool1.price;
 361 |     |         
 362 |     |         // Ensure prices never cross
 363 |     |         emit Prices(price0, price1);
 364 |     |         assert(price0 >= price1);
 365 |     |     }

 367 | *   |     function burn(int24 claimAt, uint256 positionIndex, uint128 burnPercent) public {
 368 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
 369 | *   |         positionIndex = positionIndex % positions.length;
 370 |     |         Position memory pos = positions[positionIndex];
 371 |     |         require(claimAt >= pos.lower && claimAt <= pos.upper);
 372 |     |         require(claimAt % tickSpacing == 0);
 373 |     |         PoolValues memory poolValues;
 374 |     | 
 375 |     |         (,PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool0, PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool1, uint128 liquidityGlobalBefore,,,) = pool.globalState();
 376 |     | 
 377 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params;
 378 |     |         params.to = pos.owner;
 379 |     |         params.burnPercent = burnPercent == 1e38 ? burnPercent : _between(burnPercent, 1e36, 1e38); //1e38;
 380 |     |         params.positionId = pos.positionId;
 381 |     |         params.claim = claimAt;
 382 |     |         params.zeroForOne = pos.zeroForOne;
 383 |     | 
 384 |     |         (, PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory lowerTick) = pool.ticks(pos.lower);
 385 |     |         (, PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory upperTick) = pool.ticks(pos.upper);
 386 |     | 
 387 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore = lowerTick.liquidityAbsolute;
 388 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore = upperTick.liquidityAbsolute;
 389 |     |         
 390 |     |         emit PositionTicks(pos.lower, pos.upper);
 391 |     |         (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionExists) = pool.getResizedTicksForBurn(params);
 392 |     |         emit BurnTicks(lower, upper, positionExists);
 393 |     | 
 394 |     |         // ACTION
 395 |     |         pool.burnLimit(params);
 396 |     |         if (!positionExists) {
 397 |     |             positions[positionIndex] = positions[positions.length - 1];
 398 |     |             delete positions[positions.length - 1];
 399 |     |         }
 400 |     |         else {
 401 |     |             // Update position data in array if not fully burned
 402 |     |             positions[positionIndex] = Position(pos.owner, pos.positionId, lower, upper, pos.zeroForOne);
 403 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed
 404 |     |             assert(lower < upper);
 405 |     |             // Ensure minted ticks on proper tick spacing
 406 |     |             assert((lower % tickSpacing == 0) && (upper % tickSpacing == 0));
 407 |     |         }
 408 |     | 
 409 |     |         (, lowerTick) = pool.ticks(lower);
 410 |     |         (, upperTick) = pool.ticks(upper);
 411 |     | 
 412 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter = lowerTick.liquidityAbsolute;
 413 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter = upperTick.liquidityAbsolute;
 414 |     | 
 415 |     |         (,pool0, pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter,,,) = pool.globalState();
 416 |     |         uint160 price0 = pool0.price;
 417 |     |         uint160 price1 = pool1.price;
 418 |     |         
 419 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
 420 |     | 
 421 |     |         // Ensure prices never cross
 422 |     |         emit Prices(price0, price1);
 423 |     |         assert(price0 >= price1);
 424 |     | 
 425 |     |         // Ensure liquidityGlobal is decremented after burn
 426 |     |         emit LiquidityGlobal(liquidityGlobalBefore, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter);
 427 |     |         assert((poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter <= liquidityGlobalBefore));
 428 |     |     }

 457 |     |         else {

 460 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed

 476 | *   |     function mintThenBurnZeroLiquidityChangeVariable(uint128 amount, bool zeroForOne, int24 lower, int24 upper, uint96 mintPercent) public tickPreconditions(lower, upper) {
 477 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
 478 | *   |         mintAndApprove();
 479 | *   |         PoolValues memory poolValues;

 675 |     |     function _between(uint128 val, uint low, uint high) internal pure returns(uint128) {
 676 |     |         return uint128(low + (val % (high-low +1)));

 679 |     |     function liquidityMintedBackcalculates(uint128 amount, bool zeroForOne, int24 lower, int24 upper) tickPreconditions(lower, upper) internal {
 680 |     |         // NOTE: Do not use the exact inputs of this function for POCs, use the inputs after the input validation
 681 |     |         amount = amount + 1e5 + 1;
 682 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.Immutables memory immutables = pool.immutables();
 683 |     |         uint256 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(lower, immutables);
 684 |     |         uint256 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(upper, immutables);
 685 |     | 
 686 |     |         uint256 liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
 687 |     |             priceLower,
 688 |     |             priceUpper,
 689 |     |             zeroForOne ? priceLower : priceUpper,
 690 |     |             zeroForOne ? 0 : uint256(amount),
 691 |     |             zeroForOne ? uint256(amount) : 0
 692 |     |         );
 693 |     | 
 694 |     |         (uint256 token0Amount, uint256 token1Amount) = ConstantProduct.getAmountsForLiquidity(
 695 |     |             priceLower,
 696 |     |             priceUpper,
 697 |     |             zeroForOne ? priceLower : priceUpper,
 698 |     |             liquidityMinted,
 699 |     |             true
 700 |     |         );
 701 |     | 
 702 |     |         if(zeroForOne) {
 703 |     |             emit LiquidityMinted(amount, token0Amount, zeroForOne);
 704 |     |             assert(token0Amount <= amount);
 705 |     |             
 706 |     |         }
 707 |     |         else {
 708 |     |             emit LiquidityMinted(amount, token1Amount, zeroForOne);
 709 |     |             assert(token1Amount <= amount);
 710 |     |         }
 711 |     |     }

 303 |     |     function getResizedTicksForMint(
 304 |     |         MintLimitParams memory params
 305 |     |     ) external returns (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionCreated){
 306 |     |         MintLimitCache memory cache;
 307 |     |         {
 308 |     |             cache.state = globalState;
 309 |     |             cache.constants = immutables();
 310 |     |         }
 311 |     | 
 312 |     |         try EchidnaMintLimitCall.getResizedTicks(
 313 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? positions0 : positions1,
 314 |     |             ticks,
 315 |     |             samples,
 316 |     |             rangeTickMap,
 317 |     |             limitTickMap,
 318 |     |             globalState,
 319 |     |             params,
 320 |     |             cache
 321 |     |         ) {
 322 |     |         } catch (bytes memory data) {
 323 |     |             emit SimulateMint(data);
 324 |     |             bytes4 sig;
 325 |     |             assembly {
 326 |     |                 sig := mload(add(data, 0x20))
 327 |     |             }
 328 |     |             
 329 |     |             // SimulateMint error
 330 |     |             if (sig == hex"5cc1f67b") {
 331 |     |                 (, lower, upper, positionCreated) = abi.decode(abi.encodePacked(bytes28(0), data),(bytes32,int24,int24,bool));
 332 |     |             }
 333 |     |             else {
 334 |     |                 lower = -8388608;
 335 |     |                 upper = -8388608;
 336 |     |                 positionCreated = false;
 337 |     |             }
 338 |     |         }
 339 |     |     }

 341 |     |     function getResizedTicksForBurn(
 342 |     |         BurnLimitParams memory params
 343 |     |     ) external returns (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionExists){
 344 |     |         if (params.to == address(0)) revert CollectToZeroAddress();
 345 |     |         BurnLimitCache memory cache;
 346 |     |         cache.constants = immutables();
 347 |     | 
 348 |     |         try EchidnaBurnLimitCall.getResizedTicks(
 349 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? positions0 : positions1,
 350 |     |             ticks,
 351 |     |             limitTickMap,
 352 |     |             globalState,
 353 |     |             params, 
 354 |     |             cache
 355 |     |         ) {
 356 |     |         } catch (bytes memory data) {
 357 |     |             bytes4 sig;
 358 |     |             assembly {
 359 |     |                 sig := mload(add(data, 0x20))
 360 |     |             }
 361 |     |             // SimulateBurn error
 362 |     |             if (sig == hex"97dd6e0a") {
 363 |     |                 (, lower, upper, positionExists) = abi.decode(abi.encodePacked(bytes28(0), data),(bytes32,int24,int24,bool));
 364 |     |             }
 365 |     |              else {
 366 |     |                 lower = -8388608;
 367 |     |                 upper = -8388608;
 368 |     |                 positionExists = false;
 369 |     |             }
 370 |     |         }
 371 |     |     }
 372 |     | 
 373 |     |     function priceBounds(
 374 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 375 |     |     ) external pure returns (uint160, uint160) {
 376 |     |         return ConstantProduct.priceBounds(tickSpacing);
 377 |     |     }
 378 |     | 
 379 |     |     function _onlyOwner() private view {
 380 |     |         if (msg.sender != owner()) revert OwnerOnly();
 381 |     |     }
 382 |     | 
 383 |     |     function _onlyCanoncialClones() private view {
 384 |     |         // compute pool key
 385 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(original, token0(), token1(), swapFee()));
 386 |     |         
 387 |     |         // compute canonical pool address
 388 |     |         address predictedAddress = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 389 |     |             original,
 390 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 391 |     |                 owner(),
 392 |     |                 token0(),
 393 |     |                 token1(),
 394 |     |                 poolToken(),
 395 |     |                 minPrice(),
 396 |     |                 maxPrice(),
 397 |     |                 genesisTime(),
 398 |     |                 tickSpacing(),
 399 |     |                 swapFee()
 400 |     |             ),
 401 |     |             key,
 402 |     |             factory
 403 |     |         );
 404 |     |         // only allow delegateCall from canonical clones
 405 |     |         if (address(this) != predictedAddress) require(false, 'NoDelegateCall()');
 406 |     |     }
 407 |     | 
 408 |     |     function _onlyFactory() private view {
 409 |     |         if (msg.sender != factory) revert FactoryOnly();
 410 |     |     }
 411 |     | }
 412 |     |

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import './LimitPool.sol';
   5 |     | import './interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolFactory.sol';
   6 |     | import './base/events/LimitPoolFactoryEvents.sol';
   7 |     | import './interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
   8 |     | import './utils/LimitPoolErrors.sol';
   9 |     | import './libraries/solady/LibClone.sol';
  10 |     | import './libraries/math/ConstantProduct.sol';
  11 |     | 
  12 |     | contract LimitPoolFactory is 
  13 |     |     ILimitPoolFactory,
  14 |     |     PoolsharkStructs,
  15 |     |     LimitPoolFactoryEvents,
  16 |     |     LimitPoolFactoryErrors
  17 |     | {
  18 |     |     using LibClone for address;
  19 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  20 |     | 
  21 |     |     address immutable public owner;
  22 |     |     address immutable public original;
  23 |     | 
  24 |     |     constructor(
  25 |     |         address owner_
  26 |     |     ) {
  27 |     |         owner = owner_;
  28 |     |         original = address(this);
  29 |     |     }
  30 |     | 
  31 |     |     function createLimitPool(
  32 |     |         bytes32 poolType,
  33 |     |         address tokenIn,
  34 |     |         address tokenOut,
  35 |     |         uint16  swapFee,
  36 |     |         uint160 startPrice
  37 |     |     ) external override returns (
  38 |     |         address pool,
  39 |     |         address poolToken
  40 |     |     ) {
  41 |     | 
  42 |     |         // validate token pair
  43 |     |         if (tokenIn == tokenOut || tokenIn == address(0) || tokenOut == address(0)) {
  44 |     |             revert InvalidTokenAddress();
  45 |     |         }
  46 |     | 
  47 |     |         // sort tokens by address
  48 |     |         Immutables memory constants;
  49 |     |         (constants.token0, constants.token1) = tokenIn < tokenOut ? (tokenIn,  tokenOut) 
  50 |     |                                                                   : (tokenOut, tokenIn);
  51 |     | 
  52 |     |         // check if tick spacing supported
  53 |     |         constants.swapFee = swapFee;
  54 |     |         constants.tickSpacing = ILimitPoolManager(owner).feeTiers(swapFee);
  55 |     |         if (constants.tickSpacing == 0) revert FeeTierNotSupported();
  56 |     | 
  57 |     |         // check if pool type supported
  58 |     |         (
  59 |     |             address poolImpl,
  60 |     |             address tokenImpl
  61 |     |          ) = ILimitPoolManager(owner).implementations(poolType);
  62 |     |         if (poolImpl == address(0) || tokenImpl == address(0)) revert PoolTypeNotSupported();
  63 |     | 
  64 |     |         // generate key for pool
  65 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
  66 |     |             poolImpl,
  67 |     |             constants.token0,
  68 |     |             constants.token1,
  69 |     |             constants.swapFee
  70 |     |         ));
  71 |     | 
  72 |     |         // check if pool already exists
  73 |     |         if (pools[key] != address(0)) revert PoolAlreadyExists();
  74 |     | 
  75 |     |         // set immutables
  76 |     |         constants.owner = owner;
  77 |     |         constants.factory = original;
  78 |     |         constants.genesisTime = block.timestamp.toUint32();
  79 |     |         (
  80 |     |             constants.bounds.min,
  81 |     |             constants.bounds.max
  82 |     |         ) = ILimitPool(poolImpl).priceBounds(constants.tickSpacing);
  83 |     | 
  84 |     |         // take that ERC1155 contract address and pass that into pool
  85 |     |         // launch pool token
  86 |     |         constants.poolToken = tokenImpl.cloneDeterministic({
  87 |     |             salt: key,
  88 |     |             data: abi.encodePacked(
  89 |     |                 poolImpl
  90 |     |             )
  91 |     |         });
  92 |     | 
  93 |     |         // launch pool
  94 |     |         pool = poolImpl.cloneDeterministic({
  95 |     |             salt: key,
  96 |     |             data: abi.encodePacked(
  97 |     |                 constants.owner,
  98 |     |                 constants.token0,
  99 |     |                 constants.token1,
 100 |     |                 constants.poolToken,
 101 |     |                 constants.bounds.min,
 102 |     |                 constants.bounds.max,
 103 |     |                 constants.genesisTime,
 104 |     |                 constants.tickSpacing,
 105 |     |                 constants.swapFee
 106 |     |             )
 107 |     |         });
 108 |     | 
 109 |     |         // initialize pool storage
 110 |     |         ILimitPool(pool).initialize(startPrice);
 111 |     | 
 112 |     |         // save pool in mapping
 113 |     |         pools[key] = pool;
 114 |     | 
 115 |     |         emit PoolCreated(
 116 |     |             pool,
 117 |     |             poolToken,
 118 |     |             poolImpl,
 119 |     |             tokenImpl,
 120 |     |             constants.token0,
 121 |     |             constants.token1,
 122 |     |             constants.swapFee,
 123 |     |             constants.tickSpacing
 124 |     |         );
 125 |     | 
 126 |     |         return (pool, constants.poolToken);
 127 |     |     }
 128 |     | 
 129 |     |     function getLimitPool(
 130 |     |         bytes32 poolType,
 131 |     |         address tokenIn,
 132 |     |         address tokenOut,
 133 |     |         uint16 swapFee
 134 |     |     ) external view override returns (
 135 |     |         address pool,
 136 |     |         address poolToken
 137 |     |     ) {
 138 |     |         // set lexographical token address ordering
 139 |     |         address token0 = tokenIn < tokenOut ? tokenIn : tokenOut;
 140 |     |         address token1 = tokenIn < tokenOut ? tokenOut : tokenIn;
 141 |     | 
 142 |     |         // check if tick spacing supported
 143 |     |         int16 tickSpacing = ILimitPoolManager(owner).feeTiers(swapFee);
 144 |     |         if (tickSpacing == 0) revert FeeTierNotSupported();
 145 |     | 
 146 |     |         // check if pool type supported
 147 |     |         (
 148 |     |             address poolImpl,
 149 |     |             address tokenImpl
 150 |     |          ) = ILimitPoolManager(owner).implementations(poolType);
 151 |     |         if (poolImpl == address(0) || tokenImpl == address(0)) revert PoolTypeNotSupported();
 152 |     | 
 153 |     |         // generate key for pool
 154 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
 155 |     |             poolImpl,
 156 |     |             token0,
 157 |     |             token1,
 158 |     |             swapFee
 159 |     |         ));
 160 |     | 
 161 |     |         pool = pools[key];
 162 |     | 
 163 |     |         poolToken = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 164 |     |             tokenImpl,
 165 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 166 |     |                 poolImpl
 167 |     |             ),
 168 |     |             key,
 169 |     |             address(this)
 170 |     |         );
 171 |     | 
 172 |     |         return (pool, poolToken);
 173 |     |     }
 174 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.7.0) (token/ERC20/ERC20.sol)
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | pragma solidity ^0.8.0;
   5 |     | 
   6 |     | import "./IERC20.sol";
   7 |     | import "./extensions/IERC20Metadata.sol";
   8 |     | import "../../utils/Context.sol";
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | /**
  11 |     |  * @dev Implementation of the {IERC20} interface.
  12 |     |  *
  13 |     |  * This implementation is agnostic to the way tokens are created. This means
  14 |     |  * that a supply mechanism has to be added in a derived contract using {_mint}.
  15 |     |  * For a generic mechanism see {ERC20PresetMinterPauser}.
  16 |     |  *
  17 |     |  * TIP: For a detailed writeup see our guide
  18 |     |  * https://forum.zeppelin.solutions/t/how-to-implement-erc20-supply-mechanisms/226[How
  19 |     |  * to implement supply mechanisms].
  20 |     |  *
  21 |     |  * We have followed general OpenZeppelin Contracts guidelines: functions revert
  22 |     |  * instead returning `false` on failure. This behavior is nonetheless
  23 |     |  * conventional and does not conflict with the expectations of ERC20
  24 |     |  * applications.
  25 |     |  *
  26 |     |  * Additionally, an {Approval} event is emitted on calls to {transferFrom}.
  27 |     |  * This allows applications to reconstruct the allowance for all accounts just
  28 |     |  * by listening to said events. Other implementations of the EIP may not emit
  29 |     |  * these events, as it isn't required by the specification.
  30 |     |  *
  31 |     |  * Finally, the non-standard {decreaseAllowance} and {increaseAllowance}
  32 |     |  * functions have been added to mitigate the well-known issues around setting
  33 |     |  * allowances. See {IERC20-approve}.
  34 |     |  */
  35 |     | contract ERC20 is Context, IERC20, IERC20Metadata {
  36 |     |     mapping(address => uint256) private _balances;
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |     mapping(address => mapping(address => uint256)) private _allowances;
  39 |     | 
  40 |     |     uint256 private _totalSupply;
  41 |     | 
  42 |     |     string private _name;
  43 |     |     string private _symbol;
  44 |     | 
  45 |     |     /**
  46 |     |      * @dev Sets the values for {name} and {symbol}.
  47 |     |      *
  48 |     |      * The default value of {decimals} is 18. To select a different value for
  49 |     |      * {decimals} you should overload it.
  50 |     |      *
  51 |     |      * All two of these values are immutable: they can only be set once during
  52 |     |      * construction.
  53 |     |      */
  54 |     |     constructor(string memory name_, string memory symbol_) {
  55 |     |         _name = name_;
  56 |     |         _symbol = symbol_;
  57 |     |     }
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |     /**
  60 |     |      * @dev Returns the name of the token.
  61 |     |      */
  62 |     |     function name() public view virtual override returns (string memory) {
  63 |     |         return _name;
  64 |     |     }
  65 |     | 
  66 |     |     /**
  67 |     |      * @dev Returns the symbol of the token, usually a shorter version of the
  68 |     |      * name.
  69 |     |      */
  70 |     |     function symbol() public view virtual override returns (string memory) {
  71 |     |         return _symbol;
  72 |     |     }
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |     /**
  75 |     |      * @dev Returns the number of decimals used to get its user representation.
  76 |     |      * For example, if `decimals` equals `2`, a balance of `505` tokens should
  77 |     |      * be displayed to a user as `5.05` (`505 / 10 ** 2`).
  78 |     |      *
  79 |     |      * Tokens usually opt for a value of 18, imitating the relationship between
  80 |     |      * Ether and Wei. This is the value {ERC20} uses, unless this function is
  81 |     |      * overridden;
  82 |     |      *
  83 |     |      * NOTE: This information is only used for _display_ purposes: it in
  84 |     |      * no way affects any of the arithmetic of the contract, including
  85 |     |      * {IERC20-balanceOf} and {IERC20-transfer}.
  86 |     |      */
  87 |     |     function decimals() public view virtual override returns (uint8) {
  88 |     |         return 18;
  89 |     |     }
  90 |     | 
  91 |     |     /**
  92 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-totalSupply}.
  93 |     |      */
  94 |     |     function totalSupply() public view virtual override returns (uint256) {
  95 |     |         return _totalSupply;
  96 |     |     }
  97 |     | 
  98 |     |     /**
  99 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-balanceOf}.
 100 |     |      */
 101 | *   |     function balanceOf(address account) public view virtual override returns (uint256) {
 102 | *   |         return _balances[account];
 103 |     |     }
 104 |     | 
 105 |     |     /**
 106 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-transfer}.
 107 |     |      *
 108 |     |      * Requirements:
 109 |     |      *
 110 |     |      * - `to` cannot be the zero address.
 111 |     |      * - the caller must have a balance of at least `amount`.
 112 |     |      */
 113 |     |     function transfer(address to, uint256 amount) public virtual override returns (bool) {
 114 |     |         address owner = _msgSender();
 115 |     |         _transfer(owner, to, amount);
 116 |     |         return true;
 117 |     |     }
 118 |     | 
 119 |     |     /**
 120 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-allowance}.
 121 |     |      */
 122 | *   |     function allowance(address owner, address spender) public view virtual override returns (uint256) {
 123 | *   |         return _allowances[owner][spender];
 124 |     |     }
 125 |     | 
 126 |     |     /**
 127 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-approve}.
 128 |     |      *
 129 |     |      * NOTE: If `amount` is the maximum `uint256`, the allowance is not updated on
 130 |     |      * `transferFrom`. This is semantically equivalent to an infinite approval.
 131 |     |      *
 132 |     |      * Requirements:
 133 |     |      *
 134 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 135 |     |      */
 136 | *   |     function approve(address spender, uint256 amount) public virtual override returns (bool) {
 137 | *   |         address owner = _msgSender();
 138 | *   |         _approve(owner, spender, amount);
 139 | *   |         return true;
 140 |     |     }
 141 |     | 
 142 |     |     /**
 143 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-transferFrom}.
 144 |     |      *
 145 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event indicating the updated allowance. This is not
 146 |     |      * required by the EIP. See the note at the beginning of {ERC20}.
 147 |     |      *
 148 |     |      * NOTE: Does not update the allowance if the current allowance
 149 |     |      * is the maximum `uint256`.
 150 |     |      *
 151 |     |      * Requirements:
 152 |     |      *
 153 |     |      * - `from` and `to` cannot be the zero address.
 154 |     |      * - `from` must have a balance of at least `amount`.
 155 |     |      * - the caller must have allowance for ``from``'s tokens of at least
 156 |     |      * `amount`.
 157 |     |      */
 158 | *   |     function transferFrom(
 159 |     |         address from,
 160 |     |         address to,
 161 |     |         uint256 amount
 162 | *   |     ) public virtual override returns (bool) {
 163 | *   |         address spender = _msgSender();
 164 | *   |         _spendAllowance(from, spender, amount);
 165 | *   |         _transfer(from, to, amount);
 166 | *   |         return true;
 167 |     |     }
 168 |     | 
 169 |     |     /**
 170 |     |      * @dev Atomically increases the allowance granted to `spender` by the caller.
 171 |     |      *
 172 |     |      * This is an alternative to {approve} that can be used as a mitigation for
 173 |     |      * problems described in {IERC20-approve}.
 174 |     |      *
 175 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event indicating the updated allowance.
 176 |     |      *
 177 |     |      * Requirements:
 178 |     |      *
 179 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 180 |     |      */
 181 |     |     function increaseAllowance(address spender, uint256 addedValue) public virtual returns (bool) {
 182 |     |         address owner = _msgSender();
 183 |     |         _approve(owner, spender, allowance(owner, spender) + addedValue);
 184 |     |         return true;
 185 |     |     }
 186 |     | 
 187 |     |     /**
 188 |     |      * @dev Atomically decreases the allowance granted to `spender` by the caller.
 189 |     |      *
 190 |     |      * This is an alternative to {approve} that can be used as a mitigation for
 191 |     |      * problems described in {IERC20-approve}.
 192 |     |      *
 193 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event indicating the updated allowance.
 194 |     |      *
 195 |     |      * Requirements:
 196 |     |      *
 197 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 198 |     |      * - `spender` must have allowance for the caller of at least
 199 |     |      * `subtractedValue`.
 200 |     |      */
 201 |     |     function decreaseAllowance(address spender, uint256 subtractedValue) public virtual returns (bool) {
 202 |     |         address owner = _msgSender();
 203 |     |         uint256 currentAllowance = allowance(owner, spender);
 204 |     |         require(currentAllowance >= subtractedValue, "ERC20: decreased allowance below zero");
 205 |     |         unchecked {
 206 |     |             _approve(owner, spender, currentAllowance - subtractedValue);
 207 |     |         }
 208 |     | 
 209 |     |         return true;
 210 |     |     }
 211 |     | 
 212 |     |     /**
 213 |     |      * @dev Moves `amount` of tokens from `from` to `to`.
 214 |     |      *
 215 |     |      * This internal function is equivalent to {transfer}, and can be used to
 216 |     |      * e.g. implement automatic token fees, slashing mechanisms, etc.
 217 |     |      *
 218 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event.
 219 |     |      *
 220 |     |      * Requirements:
 221 |     |      *
 222 |     |      * - `from` cannot be the zero address.
 223 |     |      * - `to` cannot be the zero address.
 224 |     |      * - `from` must have a balance of at least `amount`.
 225 |     |      */
 226 | *   |     function _transfer(
 227 |     |         address from,
 228 |     |         address to,
 229 |     |         uint256 amount
 230 | *   |     ) internal virtual {
 231 | *   |         require(from != address(0), "ERC20: transfer from the zero address");
 232 | *   |         require(to != address(0), "ERC20: transfer to the zero address");
 233 |     | 
 234 | *   |         _beforeTokenTransfer(from, to, amount);
 235 |     | 
 236 | *   |         uint256 fromBalance = _balances[from];
 237 | *   |         require(fromBalance >= amount, "ERC20: transfer amount exceeds balance");
 238 |     |         unchecked {
 239 | *   |             _balances[from] = fromBalance - amount;
 240 |     |         }
 241 | *   |         _balances[to] += amount;
 242 |     | 
 243 | *   |         emit Transfer(from, to, amount);
 244 |     | 
 245 | *   |         _afterTokenTransfer(from, to, amount);
 246 |     |     }
 247 |     | 
 248 |     |     /** @dev Creates `amount` tokens and assigns them to `account`, increasing
 249 |     |      * the total supply.
 250 |     |      *
 251 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event with `from` set to the zero address.
 252 |     |      *
 253 |     |      * Requirements:
 254 |     |      *
 255 |     |      * - `account` cannot be the zero address.
 256 |     |      */
 257 | *   |     function _mint(address account, uint256 amount) internal virtual {
 258 | *   |         require(account != address(0), "ERC20: mint to the zero address");
 259 |     | 
 260 | *   |         _beforeTokenTransfer(address(0), account, amount);
 261 |     | 
 262 | *   |         _totalSupply += amount;
 263 | *   |         _balances[account] += amount;
 264 | *   |         emit Transfer(address(0), account, amount);
 265 |     | 
 266 | *   |         _afterTokenTransfer(address(0), account, amount);
 267 |     |     }
 268 |     | 
 269 |     |     /**
 270 |     |      * @dev Destroys `amount` tokens from `account`, reducing the
 271 |     |      * total supply.
 272 |     |      *
 273 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event with `to` set to the zero address.
 274 |     |      *
 275 |     |      * Requirements:
 276 |     |      *
 277 |     |      * - `account` cannot be the zero address.
 278 |     |      * - `account` must have at least `amount` tokens.
 279 |     |      */
 280 |     |     function _burn(address account, uint256 amount) internal virtual {
 281 |     |         require(account != address(0), "ERC20: burn from the zero address");
 282 |     | 
 283 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(account, address(0), amount);
 284 |     | 
 285 |     |         uint256 accountBalance = _balances[account];
 286 |     |         require(accountBalance >= amount, "ERC20: burn amount exceeds balance");
 287 |     |         unchecked {
 288 |     |             _balances[account] = accountBalance - amount;
 289 |     |         }
 290 |     |         _totalSupply -= amount;
 291 |     | 
 292 |     |         emit Transfer(account, address(0), amount);
 293 |     | 
 294 |     |         _afterTokenTransfer(account, address(0), amount);
 295 |     |     }
 296 |     | 
 297 |     |     /**
 298 |     |      * @dev Sets `amount` as the allowance of `spender` over the `owner` s tokens.
 299 |     |      *
 300 |     |      * This internal function is equivalent to `approve`, and can be used to
 301 |     |      * e.g. set automatic allowances for certain subsystems, etc.
 302 |     |      *
 303 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event.
 304 |     |      *
 305 |     |      * Requirements:
 306 |     |      *
 307 |     |      * - `owner` cannot be the zero address.
 308 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 309 |     |      */
 310 | *   |     function _approve(
 311 |     |         address owner,
 312 |     |         address spender,
 313 |     |         uint256 amount
 314 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 315 | *   |         require(owner != address(0), "ERC20: approve from the zero address");
 316 | *   |         require(spender != address(0), "ERC20: approve to the zero address");
 317 |     | 
 318 | *   |         _allowances[owner][spender] = amount;
 319 | *   |         emit Approval(owner, spender, amount);
 320 |     |     }
 321 |     | 
 322 |     |     /**
 323 |     |      * @dev Updates `owner` s allowance for `spender` based on spent `amount`.
 324 |     |      *
 325 |     |      * Does not update the allowance amount in case of infinite allowance.
 326 |     |      * Revert if not enough allowance is available.
 327 |     |      *
 328 |     |      * Might emit an {Approval} event.
 329 |     |      */
 330 | *   |     function _spendAllowance(
 331 |     |         address owner,
 332 |     |         address spender,
 333 |     |         uint256 amount
 334 | *   |     ) internal virtual {
 335 | *   |         uint256 currentAllowance = allowance(owner, spender);
 336 | *   |         if (currentAllowance != type(uint256).max) {
 337 | *   |             require(currentAllowance >= amount, "ERC20: insufficient allowance");
 338 |     |             unchecked {
 339 | *   |                 _approve(owner, spender, currentAllowance - amount);
 340 |     |             }
 341 |     |         }
 342 |     |     }
 343 |     | 
 344 |     |     /**
 345 |     |      * @dev Hook that is called before any transfer of tokens. This includes
 346 |     |      * minting and burning.
 347 |     |      *
 348 |     |      * Calling conditions:
 349 |     |      *
 350 |     |      * - when `from` and `to` are both non-zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens
 351 |     |      * will be transferred to `to`.
 352 |     |      * - when `from` is zero, `amount` tokens will be minted for `to`.
 353 |     |      * - when `to` is zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens will be burned.
 354 |     |      * - `from` and `to` are never both zero.
 355 |     |      *
 356 |     |      * To learn more about hooks, head to xref:ROOT:extending-contracts.adoc#using-hooks[Using Hooks].
 357 |     |      */
 358 | *   |     function _beforeTokenTransfer(
 359 |     |         address from,
 360 |     |         address to,
 361 |     |         uint256 amount
 362 |     |     ) internal virtual {}
 363 |     | 
 364 |     |     /**
 365 |     |      * @dev Hook that is called after any transfer of tokens. This includes
 366 |     |      * minting and burning.
 367 |     |      *
 368 |     |      * Calling conditions:
 369 |     |      *
 370 |     |      * - when `from` and `to` are both non-zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens
 371 |     |      * has been transferred to `to`.
 372 |     |      * - when `from` is zero, `amount` tokens have been minted for `to`.
 373 |     |      * - when `to` is zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens have been burned.
 374 |     |      * - `from` and `to` are never both zero.
 375 |     |      *
 376 |     |      * To learn more about hooks, head to xref:ROOT:extending-contracts.adoc#using-hooks[Using Hooks].
 377 |     |      */
 378 | *   |     function _afterTokenTransfer(
 379 |     |         address from,
 380 |     |         address to,
 381 |     |         uint256 amount
 382 |     |     ) internal virtual {}
 383 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.6.0) (token/ERC20/IERC20.sol)
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | pragma solidity ^0.8.0;
  5 |     | 
  6 |     | /**
  7 |     |  * @dev Interface of the ERC20 standard as defined in the EIP.
  8 |     |  */
  9 |     | interface IERC20 {
 10 |     |     /**
 11 |     |      * @dev Emitted when `value` tokens are moved from one account (`from`) to
 12 |     |      * another (`to`).
 13 |     |      *
 14 |     |      * Note that `value` may be zero.
 15 |     |      */
 16 |     |     event Transfer(address indexed from, address indexed to, uint256 value);
 17 |     | 
 18 |     |     /**
 19 |     |      * @dev Emitted when the allowance of a `spender` for an `owner` is set by
 20 |     |      * a call to {approve}. `value` is the new allowance.
 21 |     |      */
 22 |     |     event Approval(address indexed owner, address indexed spender, uint256 value);
 23 |     | 
 24 |     |     /**
 25 |     |      * @dev Returns the amount of tokens in existence.
 26 |     |      */
 27 |     |     function totalSupply() external view returns (uint256);
 28 |     | 
 29 |     |     /**
 30 |     |      * @dev Returns the amount of tokens owned by `account`.
 31 |     |      */
 32 |     |     function balanceOf(address account) external view returns (uint256);
 33 |     | 
 34 |     |     /**
 35 |     |      * @dev Moves `amount` tokens from the caller's account to `to`.
 36 |     |      *
 37 |     |      * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the operation succeeded.
 38 |     |      *
 39 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event.
 40 |     |      */
 41 |     |     function transfer(address to, uint256 amount) external returns (bool);
 42 |     | 
 43 |     |     /**
 44 |     |      * @dev Returns the remaining number of tokens that `spender` will be
 45 |     |      * allowed to spend on behalf of `owner` through {transferFrom}. This is
 46 |     |      * zero by default.
 47 |     |      *
 48 |     |      * This value changes when {approve} or {transferFrom} are called.
 49 |     |      */
 50 |     |     function allowance(address owner, address spender) external view returns (uint256);
 51 |     | 
 52 |     |     /**
 53 |     |      * @dev Sets `amount` as the allowance of `spender` over the caller's tokens.
 54 |     |      *
 55 |     |      * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the operation succeeded.
 56 |     |      *
 57 |     |      * IMPORTANT: Beware that changing an allowance with this method brings the risk
 58 |     |      * that someone may use both the old and the new allowance by unfortunate
 59 |     |      * transaction ordering. One possible solution to mitigate this race
 60 |     |      * condition is to first reduce the spender's allowance to 0 and set the
 61 |     |      * desired value afterwards:
 62 |     |      * https://github.com/ethereum/EIPs/issues/20#issuecomment-263524729
 63 |     |      *
 64 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event.
 65 |     |      */
 66 |     |     function approve(address spender, uint256 amount) external returns (bool);
 67 |     | 
 68 |     |     /**
 69 |     |      * @dev Moves `amount` tokens from `from` to `to` using the
 70 |     |      * allowance mechanism. `amount` is then deducted from the caller's
 71 |     |      * allowance.
 72 |     |      *
 73 |     |      * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the operation succeeded.
 74 |     |      *
 75 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event.
 76 |     |      */
 77 |     |     function transferFrom(
 78 |     |         address from,
 79 |     |         address to,
 80 |     |         uint256 amount
 81 |     |     ) external returns (bool);
 82 |     | }
 83 |     |

  9 |     | /**
 10 |     |  * @dev Extension of {ERC20} that allows token holders to destroy both their own
 11 |     |  * tokens and those that they have an allowance for, in a way that can be
 12 |     |  * recognized off-chain (via event analysis).
 13 |     |  */
 14 |     | abstract contract ERC20Burnable is Context, ERC20 {
 15 |     |     /**
 16 |     |      * @dev Destroys `amount` tokens from the caller.
 17 |     |      *
 18 |     |      * See {ERC20-_burn}.
 19 |     |      */
 20 |     |     function burn(uint256 amount) public virtual {
 21 |     |         _burn(_msgSender(), amount);
 22 |     |     }
 23 |     | 
 24 |     |     /**
 25 |     |      * @dev Destroys `amount` tokens from `account`, deducting from the caller's
 26 |     |      * allowance.
 27 |     |      *
 28 |     |      * See {ERC20-_burn} and {ERC20-allowance}.
 29 |     |      *
 30 |     |      * Requirements:
 31 |     |      *
 32 |     |      * - the caller must have allowance for ``accounts``'s tokens of at least
 33 |     |      * `amount`.
 34 |     |      */
 35 |     |     function burnFrom(address account, uint256 amount) public virtual {

 37 |     |         _burn(account, amount);
 38 |     |     }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/openzeppelin/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.9.0) (security/ReentrancyGuard.sol)
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
  5 |     | 
  6 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
  7 |     | 
  8 |     | /**
  9 |     |  * @dev Contract module that helps prevent reentrant calls to a function.
 10 |     |  *
 11 |     |  * Inheriting from `ReentrancyGuard` will make the {nonReentrant} modifier
 12 |     |  * available, which can be applied to functions to make sure there are no nested
 13 |     |  * (reentrant) calls to them.
 14 |     |  *
 15 |     |  * Note that because there is a single `nonReentrant` guard, functions marked as
 16 |     |  * `nonReentrant` may not call one another. This can be worked around by making
 17 |     |  * those functions `private`, and then adding `external` `nonReentrant` entry
 18 |     |  * points to them.
 19 |     |  *
 20 |     |  * TIP: If you would like to learn more about reentrancy and alternative ways
 21 |     |  * to protect against it, check out our blog post
 22 |     |  * https://blog.openzeppelin.com/reentrancy-after-istanbul/[Reentrancy After Istanbul].
 23 |     |  */
 24 |     | abstract contract ReentrancyGuard is PoolsharkStructs {
 25 |     |     // Booleans are more expensive than uint256 or any type that takes up a full
 26 |     |     // word because each write operation emits an extra SLOAD to first read the
 27 |     |     // slot's contents, replace the bits taken up by the boolean, and then write
 28 |     |     // back. This is the compiler's defense against contract upgrades and
 29 |     |     // pointer aliasing, and it cannot be disabled.
 30 |     | 
 31 |     |     // The values being non-zero value makes deployment a bit more expensive,
 32 |     |     // but in exchange the refund on every call to nonReentrant will be lower in
 33 |     |     // amount. Since refunds are capped to a percentage of the total
 34 |     |     // transaction's gas, it is best to keep them low in cases like this one, to
 35 |     |     // increase the likelihood of the full refund coming into effect.
 36 |     |     uint8 private constant _NOT_ENTERED = 1;
 37 |     |     uint8 private constant _ENTERED = 2;
 38 |     | 
 39 |     |     /**
 40 |     |      * @dev Unauthorized reentrant call.
 41 |     |      */
 42 |     |     error ReentrancyGuardReentrantCall();
 43 |     | 
 44 |     |     /**
 45 |     |      * @dev Unauthorized read-only reentrant call.
 46 |     |      */
 47 |     |     error ReentrancyGuardReadOnlyReentrantCall();
 48 |     | 
 49 |     |     /**
 50 |     |      * @dev Reentrant state invalid.
 51 |     |      */
 52 |     |     error ReentrancyGuardInvalidState();
 53 |     | 
 54 |     |     /**
 55 |     |      * @dev Prevents a contract from calling itself, directly or indirectly.
 56 |     |      * Calling a `nonReentrant` function from another `nonReentrant`
 57 |     |      * function is not supported. It is possible to prevent this from happening
 58 |     |      * by making the `nonReentrant` function external, and making it call a
 59 |     |      * `private` function that does the actual work.
 60 |     |      */
 61 |     |     modifier nonReentrant(GlobalState storage state) {
 62 |     |         _nonReentrantBefore(state);
 63 |     |         _;
 64 |     |         _nonReentrantAfter(state);
 65 |     |     }
 66 |     | 
 67 |     |     function _nonReentrantBefore(GlobalState storage state) private {
 68 |     |         // On the first call to nonReentrant, _status will be _NOT_ENTERED
 69 |     |         if (state.unlocked == _ENTERED) {
 70 |     |             revert ReentrancyGuardReentrantCall();
 71 |     |         }
 72 |     | 
 73 |     |         // Any calls to nonReentrant after this point will fail
 74 |     |         state.unlocked = _ENTERED;
 75 |     |     }
 76 |     | 
 77 |     |     function _nonReentrantAfter(GlobalState storage state) private {
 78 |     |         if (state.unlocked != _ENTERED) revert ReentrancyGuardInvalidState();
 79 |     |         // By storing the original value once again, a refund is triggered (see
 80 |     |         // https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-2200)
 81 |     |         state.unlocked = _NOT_ENTERED;
 82 |     |     }
 83 |     | 
 84 |     |     /**
 85 |     |      * @dev Returns true if the reentrancy guard is currently set to "entered", which indicates there is a
 86 |     |      * `nonReentrant` function in the call stack.
 87 |     |      */
 88 |     |     function _reentrancyGuardEntered(GlobalState storage state) internal view returns (bool) {
 89 |     |         return state.unlocked == _ENTERED;
 90 |     |     }
 91 |     | }

 132 |     |     }

  10 |     | library Samples {
  11 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  12 |     | 
  13 |     |     uint8 internal constant TIME_DELTA_MAX = 6;
  14 |     | 
  15 |     |     error InvalidSampleLength();
  16 |     |     error SampleArrayUninitialized();
  17 |     |     error SampleLengthNotAvailable();
  18 |     | 
  19 |     |     event SampleRecorded(
  20 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccum,
  21 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum
  22 |     |     );
  23 |     | 
  24 |     |     event SampleLengthIncreased(
  25 |     |         uint16 sampleLengthNext
  26 |     |     );
  27 |     | 
  28 |     |     function initialize(
  29 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  30 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangePoolState memory state
  31 |     |     ) internal returns (
  32 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangePoolState memory
  33 |     |     )
  34 |     |     {
  35 |     |         samples[0] = PoolsharkStructs.Sample({
  36 |     |             blockTimestamp: uint32(block.timestamp),
  37 |     |             tickSecondsAccum: 0,
  38 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum: 0
  39 |     |         });
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |         state.samples.length = 1;
  42 |     |         state.samples.lengthNext = 5;
  43 |     | 
  44 |     |         return state;
  45 |     |         /// @dev - TWAP length of 5 is safer for oracle manipulation
  46 |     |     }
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |     function save(
  49 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  50 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SampleState memory sampleState,
  51 |     |         uint128 startLiquidity, /// @dev - liquidity from start of block
  52 |     |         int24  tick
  53 |     |     ) internal returns (
  54 |     |         uint16 sampleIndexNew,
  55 |     |         uint16 sampleLengthNew
  56 |     |     ) {
  57 |     |         // grab the latest sample
  58 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory newSample = samples[sampleState.index];
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         // early return if timestamp has not advanced 2 seconds
  61 |     |         if (newSample.blockTimestamp + 2 > uint32(block.timestamp))
  62 |     |             return (sampleState.index, sampleState.length);
  63 |     | 
  64 |     |         if (sampleState.lengthNext > sampleState.length
  65 |     |             && sampleState.index == (sampleState.length - 1)) {
  66 |     |             // increase sampleLengthNew if old size exceeded
  67 |     |             sampleLengthNew = sampleState.lengthNext;
  68 |     |         } else {
  69 |     |             sampleLengthNew = sampleState.length;
  70 |     |         }
  71 |     |         sampleIndexNew = (sampleState.index + 1) % sampleLengthNew;
  72 |     |         samples[sampleIndexNew] = _build(newSample, uint32(block.timestamp), tick, startLiquidity);
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |         emit SampleRecorded(
  75 |     |             samples[sampleIndexNew].tickSecondsAccum,
  76 |     |             samples[sampleIndexNew].secondsPerLiquidityAccum
  77 |     |         );
  78 |     |     }
  79 |     | 
  80 |     |     function expand(
  81 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  82 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangePoolState storage pool,
  83 |     |         uint16 sampleLengthNext
  84 |     |     ) internal {
  85 |     |         if (sampleLengthNext <= pool.samples.lengthNext) return ;
  86 |     |         for (uint16 i = pool.samples.lengthNext; i < sampleLengthNext; i++) {
  87 |     |             samples[i].blockTimestamp = 1;
  88 |     |         }
  89 |     |         pool.samples.lengthNext = sampleLengthNext;
  90 |     |         emit SampleLengthIncreased(sampleLengthNext);
  91 |     |     }
  92 |     | 
  93 |     |     function get(
  94 |     |         address pool,
  95 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams memory params
  96 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  97 |     |         int56[]   memory tickSecondsAccum,
  98 |     |         uint160[] memory secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
  99 |     |         uint160 averagePrice,
 100 |     |         uint128 averageLiquidity,
 101 |     |         int24 averageTick
 102 |     |     ) {
 103 |     |         if (params.sampleLength == 0) require(false, 'InvalidSampleLength()');
 104 |     |         if (params.secondsAgo.length == 0) require(false, 'SecondsAgoArrayEmpty()');
 105 |     |         uint256 size = params.secondsAgo.length > 1 ? params.secondsAgo.length : 2;
 106 |     |         uint32[] memory secondsAgo = new uint32[](size);
 107 |     |         if (params.secondsAgo.length == 1) {
 108 |     |             secondsAgo = new uint32[](2);
 109 |     |             secondsAgo[0] = params.secondsAgo[0];
 110 |     |             secondsAgo[1] = params.secondsAgo[0] + 2;
 111 |     |         }
 112 |     |         else secondsAgo = params.secondsAgo;
 113 |     | 
 114 |     |         if (secondsAgo[0] == secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1]) require(false, 'SecondsAgoArrayValuesEqual()');
 115 |     | 
 116 |     |         tickSecondsAccum = new int56[](secondsAgo.length);
 117 |     |         secondsPerLiquidityAccum = new uint160[](secondsAgo.length);
 118 |     | 
 119 |     |         for (uint256 i = 0; i < secondsAgo.length; i++) {
 120 |     |             (
 121 |     |                 tickSecondsAccum[i],
 122 |     |                 secondsPerLiquidityAccum[i]
 123 |     |             ) = getSingle(
 124 |     |                 IPool(pool),
 125 |     |                 params,
 126 |     |                 secondsAgo[i]
 127 |     |             );
 128 |     |         }
 129 |     |         if (secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1] > secondsAgo[0]) {
 130 |     |             averageTick = int24((tickSecondsAccum[0] - tickSecondsAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1]) 
 131 |     |                                 / int32(secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1] - secondsAgo[0]));
 132 |     |             averagePrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(averageTick, params.constants);
 133 |     |             averageLiquidity = uint128((secondsPerLiquidityAccum[0] - secondsPerLiquidityAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1]) 
 134 |     |                                     * (secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1] - secondsAgo[0]));
 135 |     |         } else {
 136 |     |             averageTick = int24((tickSecondsAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1] - tickSecondsAccum[0]) 
 137 |     |                                 / int32(secondsAgo[0] - secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1]));
 138 |     |             averagePrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(averageTick, params.constants);
 139 |     |             averageLiquidity = uint128((secondsPerLiquidityAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1] - secondsPerLiquidityAccum[0]) 
 140 |     |                                     * (secondsAgo[0] - secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1]));
 141 |     |         }
 142 |     |     }
