 144 |     |     function _poolSample(
 145 |     |         IPool pool,
 146 |     |         uint256 sampleIndex
 147 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 148 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory
 149 |     |     ) {
 150 |     |         (
 151 |     |             uint32 blockTimestamp,
 152 |     |             int56 tickSecondsAccum,
 153 |     |             uint160 liquidityPerSecondsAccum
 154 |     |         ) = pool.samples(sampleIndex);
 155 |     | 
 156 |     |         return PoolsharkStructs.Sample(
 157 |     |             blockTimestamp,
 158 |     |             tickSecondsAccum,
 159 |     |             liquidityPerSecondsAccum
 160 |     |         );
 161 |     |     }
 162 |     | 
 163 |     |     function getSingle(
 164 |     |         IPool pool,
 165 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams memory params,
 166 |     |         uint32 secondsAgo
 167 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 168 |     |         int56   tickSecondsAccum,
 169 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 170 |     |     ) {
 171 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory latest = _poolSample(pool, params.sampleIndex);
 172 |     | 
 173 |     |         if (secondsAgo == 0) {
 174 |     |             if (latest.blockTimestamp != uint32(block.timestamp)) {
 175 |     |                 latest = _build(
 176 |     |                     latest,
 177 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 178 |     |                     params.tick,
 179 |     |                     params.liquidity
 180 |     |                 );
 181 |     |             } 
 182 |     |             return (
 183 |     |                 latest.tickSecondsAccum,
 184 |     |                 latest.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 185 |     |             );
 186 |     |         }
 187 |     | 
 188 |     |         uint32 targetTime = uint32(block.timestamp) - secondsAgo;
 189 |     | 
 190 |     |         // should be getting samples
 191 |     |         (
 192 |     |             RangePoolStructs.Sample memory firstSample,
 193 |     |             RangePoolStructs.Sample memory secondSample
 194 |     |         ) = _getAdjacentSamples(
 195 |     |                 pool,
 196 |     |                 latest,
 197 |     |                 params,
 198 |     |                 targetTime
 199 |     |         );
 200 |     | 
 201 |     |         if (targetTime == firstSample.blockTimestamp) {
 202 |     |             // first sample
 203 |     |             return (
 204 |     |                 firstSample.tickSecondsAccum,
 205 |     |                 firstSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 206 |     |             );
 207 |     |         } else if (targetTime == secondSample.blockTimestamp) {
 208 |     |             // second sample
 209 |     |             return (
 210 |     |                 secondSample.tickSecondsAccum,
 211 |     |                 secondSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 212 |     |             );
 213 |     |         } else {
 214 |     |             // average two samples
 215 |     |             int32 sampleTimeDelta = int32(secondSample.blockTimestamp - firstSample.blockTimestamp);
 216 |     |             int56 targetDelta = int56(int32(targetTime - firstSample.blockTimestamp));
 217 |     |             return (
 218 |     |                 firstSample.tickSecondsAccum +
 219 |     |                     ((secondSample.tickSecondsAccum - firstSample.tickSecondsAccum) 
 220 |     |                     / sampleTimeDelta)
 221 |     |                     * targetDelta,
 222 |     |                 firstSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum +
 223 |     |                     uint160(
 224 |     |                         (uint256(
 225 |     |                             secondSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum - firstSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 226 |     |                         ) 
 227 |     |                         * uint256(uint56(targetDelta))) 
 228 |     |                         / uint32(sampleTimeDelta)
 229 |     |                     )
 230 |     |             );
 231 |     |         }
 232 |     |     }
 233 |     | 
 234 |     |     function getLatest(
 235 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 236 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
 237 |     |         uint256 liquidity
 238 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 239 |     |         uint160 latestPrice,
 240 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 241 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccum
 242 |     |     ) {
 243 |     |         uint32 timeDelta = timeElapsed(constants);
 244 |     |         (
 245 |     |             tickSecondsAccum,
 246 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 247 |     |         ) = getSingle(
 248 |     |                 IPool(address(this)), 
 249 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
 250 |     |                     state.pool.samples.index,
 251 |     |                     state.pool.samples.length,
 252 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 253 |     |                     new uint32[](2),
 254 |     |                     state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 255 |     |                     liquidity.toUint128(),
 256 |     |                     constants
 257 |     |                 ),
 258 |     |                 0
 259 |     |         );
 260 |     |         // grab older sample for dynamic fee calculation
 261 |     |         (
 262 |     |             int56 tickSecondsAccumBase,
 263 |     |         ) = Samples.getSingle(
 264 |     |                 IPool(address(this)), 
 265 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
 266 |     |                     state.pool.samples.index,
 267 |     |                     state.pool.samples.length,
 268 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 269 |     |                     new uint32[](2),
 270 |     |                     state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 271 |     |                     liquidity.toUint128(),
 272 |     |                     constants
 273 |     |                 ),
 274 |     |                 timeDelta
 275 |     |         );
 276 |     | 
 277 |     |         latestPrice = calculateLatestPrice(
 278 |     |             tickSecondsAccum,
 279 |     |             tickSecondsAccumBase,
 280 |     |             timeDelta,
 281 |     |             TIME_DELTA_MAX,
 282 |     |             constants
 283 |     |         );
 284 |     |     }
 285 |     | 
 286 |     |     function calculateLatestPrice(
 287 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccum,
 288 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccumBase,
 289 |     |         uint32 timeDelta,
 290 |     |         uint32 timeDeltaMax,
 291 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 292 |     |     ) private pure returns (
 293 |     |         uint160 averagePrice
 294 |     |     ) {
 295 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccumDiff = tickSecondsAccum - tickSecondsAccumBase;
 296 |     |         int24 averageTick;
 297 |     |         if (timeDelta == timeDeltaMax) {
 298 |     |             averageTick = int24(tickSecondsAccumDiff / int32(timeDelta));
 299 |     |         } else {
 300 |     |             averageTick = int24(tickSecondsAccum / int32(timeDelta));
 301 |     |         }
 302 |     |         averagePrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(averageTick, constants);
 303 |     |     }
 304 |     | 
 305 |     | 
 306 |     |     function timeElapsed(
 307 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 308 |     |     ) private view returns (
 309 |     |         uint32
 310 |     |     )    
 311 |     |     {
 312 |     |         return  uint32(block.timestamp) - constants.genesisTime >= TIME_DELTA_MAX
 313 |     |                     ? TIME_DELTA_MAX
 314 |     |                     : uint32(block.timestamp - constants.genesisTime);
 315 |     |     }
 316 |     | 
 317 |     |     function _lte(
 318 |     |         uint32 timeA,
 319 |     |         uint32 timeB
 320 |     |     ) private view returns (bool) {
 321 |     |         uint32 currentTime = uint32(block.timestamp);
 322 |     |         if (timeA <= currentTime && timeB <= currentTime) return timeA <= timeB;
 323 |     | 
 324 |     |         uint256 timeAOverflow = timeA;
 325 |     |         uint256 timeBOverflow = timeB;
 326 |     | 
 327 |     |         if (timeA <= currentTime) {
 328 |     |             timeAOverflow = timeA + 2**32;
 329 |     |         }
 330 |     |         if (timeB <= currentTime) {
 331 |     |             timeBOverflow = timeB + 2**32;
 332 |     |         }
 333 |     | 
 334 |     |         return timeAOverflow <= timeBOverflow;
 335 |     |     }
 336 |     | 
 337 |     |     function _build(
 338 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory newSample,
 339 |     |         uint32  blockTimestamp,
 340 |     |         int24   tick,
 341 |     |         uint128 liquidity
 342 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 343 |     |          RangePoolStructs.Sample memory
 344 |     |     ) {
 345 |     |         int56 timeDelta = int56(uint56(blockTimestamp - newSample.blockTimestamp));
 346 |     | 
 347 |     |         return
 348 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.Sample({
 349 |     |                 blockTimestamp: blockTimestamp,
 350 |     |                 tickSecondsAccum: newSample.tickSecondsAccum + int56(tick) * int32(timeDelta),
 351 |     |                 secondsPerLiquidityAccum: newSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum +
 352 |     |                     ((uint160(uint56(timeDelta)) << 128) / (liquidity > 0 ? liquidity : 1))
 353 |     |             });
 354 |     |     }
 355 |     | 
 356 |     |     function _binarySearch(
 357 |     |         IPool pool,
 358 |     |         uint32 targetTime,
 359 |     |         uint16 sampleIndex,
 360 |     |         uint16 sampleLength
 361 |     |     ) private view returns (
 362 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory firstSample,
 363 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory secondSample
 364 |     |     ) {
 365 |     |         uint256 oldIndex = (sampleIndex + 1) % sampleLength;
 366 |     |         uint256 newIndex = oldIndex + sampleLength - 1;             
 367 |     |         uint256 index;
 368 |     |         while (true) {
 369 |     |             // start in the middle
 370 |     |             index = (oldIndex + newIndex) / 2;
 371 |     | 
 372 |     |             // get the first sample
 373 |     |             firstSample = _poolSample(pool, index % sampleLength);
 374 |     | 
 375 |     |             // if sample is uninitialized
 376 |     |             if (firstSample.blockTimestamp == 0) {
 377 |     |                 // skip this index and continue
 378 |     |                 oldIndex = index + 1;
 379 |     |                 continue;
 380 |     |             }
 381 |     |             // else grab second sample
 382 |     |             secondSample = _poolSample(pool, (index + 1) % sampleLength);
 383 |     | 
 384 |     |             // check if target time within first and second sample
 385 |     |             bool targetAfterFirst   = _lte(firstSample.blockTimestamp, targetTime);
 386 |     |             bool targetBeforeSecond = _lte(targetTime, secondSample.blockTimestamp);
 387 |     |             if (targetAfterFirst && targetBeforeSecond) break;
 388 |     |             if (!targetAfterFirst) newIndex = index - 1;
 389 |     |             else oldIndex = index + 1;
 390 |     |         }
 391 |     |     }
 392 |     | 
 393 |     |     function _getAdjacentSamples(
 394 |     |         IPool pool,
 395 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory firstSample,
 396 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams memory params,
 397 |     |         uint32 targetTime
 398 |     |     ) private view returns (
 399 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory,
 400 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory
 401 |     |     ) {
 402 |     |         if (_lte(firstSample.blockTimestamp, targetTime)) {
 403 |     |             if (firstSample.blockTimestamp == targetTime) {
 404 |     |                 return (firstSample, PoolsharkStructs.Sample(0,0,0));
 405 |     |             } else {
 406 |     |                 return (firstSample, _build(firstSample, targetTime, params.tick, params.liquidity));
 407 |     |             }
 408 |     |         }
 409 |     |         firstSample = _poolSample(pool, (params.sampleIndex + 1) % params.sampleLength);
 410 |     |         if (firstSample.blockTimestamp == 0) {
 411 |     |             firstSample = _poolSample(pool, 0);
 412 |     |         }
 413 |     |         if(!_lte(firstSample.blockTimestamp, targetTime)) require(false, 'SampleLengthNotAvailable()');
 414 |     | 
 415 |     |         return _binarySearch(
 416 |     |             pool,
 417 |     |             targetTime,
 418 |     |             params.sampleIndex,
 419 |     |             params.sampleLength
 420 |     |         );
 421 |     |     }
 422 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/TickMap.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPLv3
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import './math/ConstantProduct.sol';
   5 |     | import '../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
   6 |     | 
   7 |     | library TickMap {
   8 |     | 
   9 |     |     error TickIndexOverflow();
  10 |     |     error TickIndexUnderflow();
  11 |     |     error TickIndexBadSpacing();
  12 |     |     error BlockIndexOverflow();
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     function get(
  15 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  16 |     |         int24 tick,
  17 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  18 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  19 |     |         bool exists
  20 |     |     ) {
  21 |     |         (
  22 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  23 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  24 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
  25 |     | 
  26 |     |         // check if bit is already set
  27 |     |         uint256 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] | 1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF);
  28 |     |         if (word == tickMap.ticks[wordIndex]) {
  29 |     |             return true;
  30 |     |         }
  31 |     |         return false;
  32 |     |     }
  33 |     | 
  34 |     |     function set(
  35 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  36 |     |         int24 tick,
  37 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  38 |     |     ) internal returns (
  39 |     |         bool exists
  40 |     |     ) {
  41 |     |         (
  42 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  43 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  44 |     |             uint256 blockIndex
  45 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
  46 |     | 
  47 |     |         // check if bit is already set
  48 |     |         uint256 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] | 1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF);
  49 |     |         if (word == tickMap.ticks[wordIndex]) {
  50 |     |             return true;
  51 |     |         }
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |         tickMap.ticks[wordIndex]     = word; 
  54 |     |         tickMap.words[blockIndex]   |= 1 << (wordIndex & 0xFF); // same as modulus 255
  55 |     |         tickMap.blocks              |= 1 << blockIndex;
  56 |     |         return false;
  57 |     |     }
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |     function unset(
  60 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  61 |     |         int24 tick,
  62 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
  63 |     |     ) internal {
  64 |     |         (
  65 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  66 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  67 |     |             uint256 blockIndex
  68 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
  69 |     | 
  70 |     |         tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] &= ~(1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF));
  71 |     |         if (tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] == 0) {
  72 |     |             tickMap.words[blockIndex] &= ~(1 << (wordIndex & 0xFF));
  73 |     |             if (tickMap.words[blockIndex] == 0) {
  74 |     |                 tickMap.blocks &= ~(1 << blockIndex);
  75 |     |             }
  76 |     |         }
  77 |     |     }
  78 |     | 
  79 |     |     function previous(
  80 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  81 |     |         int24 tick,
  82 |     |         int16 tickSpacing,
  83 |     |         bool inclusive
  84 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  85 |     |         int24 previousTick
  86 |     |     ) {
  87 |     |         unchecked {
  88 |     |             // rounds up to ensure relative position
  89 |     |             if (tick % (tickSpacing / 2) != 0 || inclusive) {
  90 |     |                 if (tick < (ConstantProduct.maxTick(tickSpacing) - tickSpacing / 2)) {
  91 |     |                     /// @dev - ensures we cross when tick >= 0
  92 |     |                     if (tick >= 0) {
  93 |     |                         tick += tickSpacing / 2;
  94 |     |                     } else if (inclusive && tick % (tickSpacing / 2) == 0) {
  95 |     |                     /// @dev - ensures we cross when tick == tickAtPrice
  96 |     |                         tick += tickSpacing / 2;
  97 |     |                     }
  98 |     |                 }
  99 |     |             }
 100 |     |             (
 101 |     |               uint256 tickIndex,
 102 |     |               uint256 wordIndex,
 103 |     |               uint256 blockIndex
 104 |     |             ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
 105 |     | 
 106 |     |             uint256 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] & ((1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF)) - 1);
 107 |     |             if (word == 0) {
 108 |     |                 uint256 block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex] & ((1 << (wordIndex & 0xFF)) - 1);
 109 |     |                 if (block_ == 0) {
 110 |     |                     uint256 blockMap = tickMap.blocks & ((1 << blockIndex) - 1);
 111 |     |                     if (blockMap == 0) return tick;
 112 |     | 
 113 |     |                     blockIndex = _msb(blockMap);
 114 |     |                     block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex];
 115 |     |                 }
 116 |     |                 wordIndex = (blockIndex << 8) | _msb(block_);
 117 |     |                 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex];
 118 |     |             }
 119 |     |             previousTick = _tick((wordIndex << 8) | _msb(word), tickSpacing);
 120 |     |         }
 121 |     |     }
 122 |     | 
 123 |     |     function next(
 124 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 125 |     |         int24 tick,
 126 |     |         int16 tickSpacing,
 127 |     |         bool inclusive
 128 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 129 |     |         int24 nextTick
 130 |     |     ) {
 131 |     |         unchecked {
 132 |     |             /// @dev - handles tickAtPrice being past tickSpacing / 2
 133 |     |             if (inclusive && tick % tickSpacing != 0) {
 134 |     |                 // e.g. tick is 5 we subtract 1 to look ahead at 5
 135 |     |                 if (tick > 0 && (tick % tickSpacing <= (tickSpacing / 2)))
 136 |     |                     tick -= 1;
 137 |     |                 // e.g. tick is -5 we subtract 1 to look ahead at -5
 138 |     |                 else if (tick < 0 && (tick % tickSpacing <= -(tickSpacing / 2)))
 139 |     |                     tick -= 1;
 140 |     |                 // e.g. tick = 7 and tickSpacing = 10 we sub 5 to look ahead at 5
 141 |     |                 // e.g. tick = -2 and tickSpacing = 10 we sub 5 to look ahead at -5
 142 |     |                 else
 143 |     |                     tick -= tickSpacing / 2;
 144 |     |             }
 145 |     |             /// @dev - handles negative ticks rounding up
 146 |     |             if (tick % (tickSpacing / 2) != 0) {
 147 |     |                 if (tick < 0)
 148 |     |                     if (tick > (ConstantProduct.minTick(tickSpacing) + tickSpacing / 2))
 149 |     |                         tick -= tickSpacing / 2;
 150 |     |             }
 151 |     |             (
 152 |     |               uint256 tickIndex,
 153 |     |               uint256 wordIndex,
 154 |     |               uint256 blockIndex
 155 |     |             ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
 156 |     |             uint256 word;
 157 |     |             if ((tickIndex & 0xFF) != 255) {
 158 |     |                 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] & ~((1 << ((tickIndex & 0xFF) + 1)) - 1);
 159 |     |             }
 160 |     |             if (word == 0) {
 161 |     |                 uint256 block_;
 162 |     |                 if ((blockIndex & 0xFF) != 255) {
 163 |     |                     block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex] & ~((1 << ((wordIndex & 0xFF) + 1)) - 1);
 164 |     |                 }
 165 |     |                 if (block_ == 0) {
 166 |     |                     uint256 blockMap = tickMap.blocks & ~((1 << blockIndex + 1) - 1);
 167 |     |                     if (blockMap == 0) return tick;
 168 |     |                     blockIndex = _lsb(blockMap);
 169 |     |                     block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex];
 170 |     |                 }
 171 |     |                 wordIndex = (blockIndex << 8) | _lsb(block_);
 172 |     |                 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex];
 173 |     |             }
 174 |     |             nextTick = _tick((wordIndex << 8) | _lsb(word), tickSpacing);
 175 |     |         }
 176 |     |     }
 177 |     | 
 178 |     |     function getIndices(
 179 |     |         int24 tick,
 180 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
 181 |     |     ) public pure returns (
 182 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
 183 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
 184 |     |             uint256 blockIndex
 185 |     |         )
 186 |     |     {
 187 |     |         unchecked {
 188 |     |             if (tick > ConstantProduct.MAX_TICK) require(false, ' TickIndexOverflow()');
 189 |     |             if (tick < ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK) require(false, 'TickIndexUnderflow()');
 190 |     |             if (tick % (tickSpacing / 2) != 0) tick = round(tick, tickSpacing / 2);
 191 |     |             tickIndex = uint256(int256((round(tick, tickSpacing / 2) 
 192 |     |                                         - round(ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK, tickSpacing / 2)) 
 193 |     |                                         / (tickSpacing / 2)));
 194 |     |             wordIndex = tickIndex >> 8;   // 2^8 ticks per word
 195 |     |             blockIndex = tickIndex >> 16; // 2^8 words per block
 196 |     |             if (blockIndex > 255) require(false, 'BlockIndexOverflow()');
 197 |     |         }
 198 |     |     }
 199 |     | 
 200 |     | 
 201 |     | 
 202 |     |     function _tick (
 203 |     |         uint256 tickIndex,
 204 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
 205 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 206 |     |         int24 tick
 207 |     |     ) {
 208 |     |         unchecked {
 209 |     |             if (tickIndex > uint24(round(ConstantProduct.MAX_TICK, tickSpacing) * 2) * 2) 
 210 |     |                 require(false, 'TickIndexOverflow()');
 211 |     |             tick = int24(int256(tickIndex) * (tickSpacing / 2) + round(ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK, tickSpacing / 2));
 212 |     |         }
 213 |     |     }
 214 |     | 
 215 |     |     function _msb(
 216 |     |         uint256 x
 217 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 218 |     |         uint8 r
 219 |     |     ) {
 220 |     |         unchecked {
 221 |     |             assert(x > 0);
 222 |     |             if (x >= 0x100000000000000000000000000000000) {
 223 |     |                 x >>= 128;
 224 |     |                 r += 128;
 225 |     |             }
 226 |     |             if (x >= 0x10000000000000000) {
 227 |     |                 x >>= 64;
 228 |     |                 r += 64;
 229 |     |             }
 230 |     |             if (x >= 0x100000000) {
 231 |     |                 x >>= 32;
 232 |     |                 r += 32;
 233 |     |             }
 234 |     |             if (x >= 0x10000) {
 235 |     |                 x >>= 16;
 236 |     |                 r += 16;
 237 |     |             }
 238 |     |             if (x >= 0x100) {
 239 |     |                 x >>= 8;
 240 |     |                 r += 8;
 241 |     |             }
 242 |     |             if (x >= 0x10) {
 243 |     |                 x >>= 4;
 244 |     |                 r += 4;
 245 |     |             }
 246 |     |             if (x >= 0x4) {
 247 |     |                 x >>= 2;
 248 |     |                 r += 2;
 249 |     |             }
 250 |     |             if (x >= 0x2) r += 1;
 251 |     |         }
 252 |     |     }
 253 |     | 
 254 |     |     function _lsb(
 255 |     |         uint256 x
 256 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 257 |     |         uint8 r
 258 |     |     ) {
 259 |     |         unchecked {
 260 |     |             assert(x > 0); // if x is 0 return 0
 261 |     |             r = 255;
 262 |     |             if (x & type(uint128).max > 0) {
 263 |     |                 r -= 128;
 264 |     |             } else {
 265 |     |                 x >>= 128;
 266 |     |             }
 267 |     |             if (x & type(uint64).max > 0) {
 268 |     |                 r -= 64;
 269 |     |             } else {
 270 |     |                 x >>= 64;
 271 |     |             }
 272 |     |             if (x & type(uint32).max > 0) {
 273 |     |                 r -= 32;
 274 |     |             } else {
 275 |     |                 x >>= 32;
 276 |     |             }
 277 |     |             if (x & type(uint16).max > 0) {
 278 |     |                 r -= 16;
 279 |     |             } else {
 280 |     |                 x >>= 16;
 281 |     |             }
 282 |     |             if (x & type(uint8).max > 0) {
 283 |     |                 r -= 8;
 284 |     |             } else {
 285 |     |                 x >>= 8;
 286 |     |             }
 287 |     |             if (x & 0xf > 0) {
 288 |     |                 r -= 4;
 289 |     |             } else {
 290 |     |                 x >>= 4;
 291 |     |             }
 292 |     |             if (x & 0x3 > 0) {
 293 |     |                 r -= 2;
 294 |     |             } else {
 295 |     |                 x >>= 2;
 296 |     |             }
 297 |     |             if (x & 0x1 > 0) r -= 1;
 298 |     |         }
 299 |     |     }
 300 |     | 
 301 |     |     function round(
 302 |     |         int24 tick,
 303 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
 304 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 305 |     |         int24 roundedTick
 306 |     |     ) {
 307 |     |         return tick / tickSpacing * tickSpacing;
 308 |     |     }
 309 |     | 
 310 |     |     function roundHalf(
 311 |     |         int24 tick,
 312 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
 313 |     |         uint256 price
 314 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 315 |     |         int24 roundedTick,
 316 |     |         uint160 roundedTickPrice
 317 |     |     ) {
 318 |     |         //pool.tickAtPrice -99.5
 319 |     |         //pool.tickAtPrice -100
 320 |     |         //-105
 321 |     |         //-95
 322 |     |         roundedTick = tick / constants.tickSpacing * constants.tickSpacing;
 323 |     |         roundedTickPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(roundedTick, constants);
 324 |     |         if (price == roundedTickPrice)
 325 |     |             return (roundedTick, roundedTickPrice);
 326 |     |         if (roundedTick > 0) {
 327 |     |             roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 328 |     |         } else if (roundedTick < 0) {
 329 |     |             if (roundedTickPrice < price)
 330 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 331 |     |             else
 332 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 333 |     |         } else {
 334 |     |             if (price > roundedTickPrice) {
 335 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 336 |     |             } else if (price < roundedTickPrice) {
 337 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 338 |     |             }
 339 |     |         }
 340 |     |     }
 341 |     | 
 342 |     |     function roundAhead(
 343 |     |         int24 tick,
 344 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
 345 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 346 |     |         uint256 price
 347 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 348 |     |         int24 roundedTick
 349 |     |     ) {
 350 |     |         roundedTick = tick / constants.tickSpacing * constants.tickSpacing;
 351 |     |         uint160 roundedTickPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(roundedTick, constants);
 352 |     |         if (price == roundedTickPrice)
 353 |     |             return roundedTick;
 354 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 355 |     |             // round up if positive
 356 |     |             if (roundedTick > 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick >= 0))
 357 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 358 |     |             else if (tick % constants.tickSpacing == 0) {
 359 |     |                 // handle price at -99.5 and tickAtPrice == -100
 360 |     |                 if (tick < 0 && roundedTickPrice < price) {
 361 |     |                     roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 362 |     |                 }
 363 |     |             }
 364 |     |         } else {
 365 |     |             // round down if negative
 366 |     |             if (roundedTick < 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick < 0))
 367 |     |             /// @dev - strictly less due to TickMath always rounding to lesser values
 368 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing;
 369 |     |         }
 370 |     |     }
 371 |     | 
 372 |     |     function roundBack(
 373 |     |         int24 tick,
 374 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
 375 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 376 |     |         uint256 price
 377 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 378 |     |         int24 roundedTick
 379 |     |     ) {
 380 |     |         roundedTick = tick / constants.tickSpacing * constants.tickSpacing;
 381 |     |         uint160 roundedTickPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(roundedTick, constants);
 382 |     |         if (price == roundedTickPrice)
 383 |     |             return roundedTick;
 384 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 385 |     |             // round down if negative
 386 |     |             if (roundedTick < 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick < 0))
 387 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing;
 388 |     |         } else {
 389 |     |             // round up if positive
 390 |     |             if (roundedTick > 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick >= 0))
 391 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 392 |     |             else if (tick % constants.tickSpacing == 0) {
 393 |     |                 // handle price at -99.5 and tickAtPrice == -100
 394 |     |                 if (tick < 0 && roundedTickPrice < price) {
 395 |     |                     roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 396 |     |                 }
 397 |     |             }
 398 |     |         }
 399 |     |     }
 400 |     | }

  55 |     |     function initialize(
  56 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  57 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  58 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  59 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
  60 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
  61 |     |         uint160 startPrice
  62 |     |     ) internal returns (
  63 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory  
  64 |     |     )
  65 |     |     {
  66 |     |         // state should only be initialized once
  67 |     |         if (state.pool0.price > 0) require (false, 'PoolAlreadyInitialized()');
  68 |     | 
  69 |     |         // initialize state
  70 |     |         state.epoch = 1;
  71 |     |         state.positionIdNext = 1;
  72 |     | 
  73 |     |         // check price bounds
  74 |     |         if (startPrice < constants.bounds.min || startPrice >= constants.bounds.max) require(false, 'StartPriceInvalid()');
  75 |     | 
  76 |     |         // initialize range ticks
  77 |     |         TickMap.set(rangeTickMap, ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  78 |     |         TickMap.set(rangeTickMap, ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  79 |     |         
  80 |     |         // initialize limit ticks
  81 |     |         TickMap.set(limitTickMap, ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  82 |     |         TickMap.set(limitTickMap, ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  83 |     | 
  84 |     |         // initialize price
  85 |     |         state.pool.price = startPrice;
  86 |     |         state.pool0.price = startPrice;
  87 |     |         state.pool1.price = startPrice;
  88 |     | 
  89 |     |         int24 startTick = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(startPrice, constants);
  90 |     |         state.pool.tickAtPrice = startTick;
  91 |     |         state.pool0.tickAtPrice = startTick;
  92 |     |         state.pool1.tickAtPrice = startTick;
  93 |     | 
  94 |     |         // intialize samples
  95 |     |         state.pool = Samples.initialize(samples, state.pool);
  96 |     | 
  97 |     |         // emit event
  98 |     |         emit Initialize(
  99 |     |             ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing),
 100 |     |             ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing),
 101 |     |             state.pool0.price,
 102 |     |             state.pool0.tickAtPrice
 103 |     |         );
 104 |     | 
 105 |     |         return state;
 106 |     |     }
 107 |     |     
 108 |     |     function swap(
 109 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 110 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
 111 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 112 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 113 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams memory params,
 114 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache
 115 |     |     ) internal returns (
 116 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 117 |     |     )
 118 |     |     {   
 119 |     |         // if price == priceAtTick
 120 |     |         // cross range tick if present
 121 |     |         // in _cross if price == priceAtTick && amountLeft == 0
 122 |     |         // don't cross the range tick
 123 |     |         // start with range price
 124 |     |         cache.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 125 |     |         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 126 |     | 
 127 |     |         cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, true);
 128 |     | 
 129 |     |         uint128 startLiquidity = cache.liquidity.toUint128();
 130 |     | 
 131 |     |         // set crossTick/crossPrice based on the best between limit and range
 132 |     |         // grab sample for accumulators
 133 |     |         cache = PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache({
 134 |     |             state: cache.state,
 135 |     |             constants: cache.constants,
 136 |     |             price: cache.price,
 137 |     |             liquidity: cache.liquidity,
 138 |     |             amountLeft: params.amount,
 139 |     |             input:  0,
 140 |     |             output: 0,
 141 |     |             crossPrice: cache.crossPrice,
 142 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum: 0,
 143 |     |             feeAmount: 0,
 144 |     |             tickSecondsAccum: 0,
 145 |     |             tickSecondsAccumBase: 0,
 146 |     |             crossTick: cache.crossTick,
 147 |     |             crossStatus: cache.crossStatus,
 148 |     |             limitActive: cache.limitActive,
 149 |     |             exactIn: params.exactIn,
 150 |     |             cross: true,
 151 |     |             averagePrice: 0
 152 |     |         });
 153 |     |         // grab latest price and sample
 154 |     |         (
 155 |     |             cache.averagePrice,
 156 |     |             cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 157 |     |             cache.tickSecondsAccum
 158 |     |          ) = Samples.getLatest(cache.state, cache.constants, cache.liquidity);
 159 |     | 
 160 |     |         // grab latest sample and store in cache for _cross
 161 |     |         while (cache.cross) {
 162 |     |             // handle price being at cross tick
 163 |     |             cache = _quoteSingle(cache, params.priceLimit, params.zeroForOne);
 164 |     |             if (cache.cross) {
 165 |     |                 cache = _cross(
 166 |     |                     ticks,
 167 |     |                     rangeTickMap,
 168 |     |                     limitTickMap,
 169 |     |                     cache,
 170 |     |                     params
 171 |     |                 );
 172 |     |             }
 173 |     |         }
 174 |     |         /// @dev - write oracle entry after start of block
 175 |     |         (
 176 |     |             cache.state.pool.samples.index,
 177 |     |             cache.state.pool.samples.length
 178 |     |         ) = Samples.save(
 179 |     |             samples,
 180 |     |             cache.state.pool.samples,
 181 |     |             startLiquidity,
 182 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice
 183 |     |         );
 184 |     |         // pool liquidity should be updated along the way
 185 |     |         cache.state.pool.price = cache.price.toUint160();
 186 |     | 
 187 |     |         if (cache.price != cache.crossPrice) {
 188 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(cache.price.toUint160(), cache.constants);
 189 |     |         } else {
 190 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice = cache.crossTick;
 191 |     |         }
 192 |     |         if (cache.limitActive) {
 193 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 194 |     |                 cache.state.pool1.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 195 |     |                 cache.state.pool1.tickAtPrice = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 196 |     |             } else {
 197 |     |                 cache.state.pool0.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 198 |     |                 cache.state.pool0.tickAtPrice = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 199 |     |             }
 200 |     |         }
 201 |     |         emit Swap(
 202 |     |             params.to,
 203 |     |             cache.input,
 204 |     |             cache.output,
 205 |     |             cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0,
 206 |     |             cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1,
 207 |     |             cache.price.toUint160(),
 208 |     |             cache.liquidity.toUint128(),
 209 |     |             cache.feeAmount,
 210 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 211 |     |             params.zeroForOne,
 212 |     |             params.exactIn
 213 |     |         );
 214 |     |         return cache;
 215 |     |     }
 216 |     | 
 217 |     |     function quote(
 218 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 219 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 220 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 221 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.QuoteParams memory params,
 222 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache
 223 |     |     ) internal returns (
 224 |     |         uint256,
 225 |     |         uint256,
 226 |     |         uint160
 227 |     |     ) {
 228 |     |         // start with range price
 229 |     |         cache.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 230 |     |         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 231 |     | 
 232 |     |         cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, true);
 233 |     |         
 234 |     |         // set crossTick/crossPrice based on the best between limit and range
 235 |     |         // grab sample for accumulators
 236 |     |         cache = PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache({
 237 |     |             state: cache.state,
 238 |     |             constants: cache.constants,
 239 |     |             price: cache.price,
 240 |     |             liquidity: cache.liquidity,
 241 |     |             amountLeft: params.amount,
 242 |     |             input:  0,
 243 |     |             output: 0,
 244 |     |             crossPrice: cache.crossPrice,
 245 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum: 0,
 246 |     |             feeAmount: 0,
 247 |     |             tickSecondsAccum: 0,
 248 |     |             tickSecondsAccumBase: 0,
 249 |     |             crossTick: cache.crossTick,
 250 |     |             crossStatus: cache.crossStatus,
 251 |     |             limitActive: cache.limitActive,
 252 |     |             exactIn: params.exactIn,
 253 |     |             cross: true,
 254 |     |             averagePrice: 0
 255 |     |         });
 256 |     |         // grab latest price and sample
 257 |     |         (
 258 |     |             cache.averagePrice,
 259 |     |             cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 260 |     |             cache.tickSecondsAccum
 261 |     |          ) = Samples.getLatest(cache.state, cache.constants, cache.liquidity);
 262 |     |         while (cache.cross) {
 263 |     |             cache = _quoteSingle(cache, params.priceLimit, params.zeroForOne);
 264 |     |             if (cache.cross) {
 265 |     |                 cache = _pass(
 266 |     |                     ticks,
 267 |     |                     rangeTickMap,
 268 |     |                     limitTickMap,
 269 |     |                     cache,
 270 |     |                     params
 271 |     |                 );
 272 |     |             }
 273 |     |         }
 274 |     |         return (
 275 |     |             cache.input,
 276 |     |             cache.output,
 277 |     |             cache.price.toUint160()
 278 |     |         );
 279 |     |     }
 280 |     | 
 281 |     |     function _quoteSingle(
 282 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 283 |     |         uint160 priceLimit,
 284 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 285 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 286 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 287 |     |     ) {
 288 |     |         if ((zeroForOne ? priceLimit >= cache.price
 289 |     |                         : priceLimit <= cache.price) ||
 290 |     |             (zeroForOne && cache.price == cache.constants.bounds.min) ||
 291 |     |             (!zeroForOne && cache.price == cache.constants.bounds.max) ||
 292 |     |             (cache.amountLeft == 0 && cache.liquidity > 0))
 293 |     |         {
 294 |     |             cache.cross = false;
 295 |     |             return cache;
 296 |     |         }
 297 |     |         uint256 nextPrice = cache.crossPrice;
 298 |     |          uint256 amountIn; uint256 amountOut;
 299 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 300 |     |             // Trading token 0 (x) for token 1 (y).
 301 |     |             // price  is decreasing.
 302 |     |             if (nextPrice < priceLimit) {
 303 |     |                 nextPrice = priceLimit;
 304 |     |             }
 305 |     |             uint256 amountMax = cache.exactIn ? ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, true)
 306 |     |                                               : ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, false);
 307 |     |             if (cache.amountLeft < amountMax) {
 308 |     |                 // calculate price after swap
 309 |     |                 uint256 newPrice = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(
 310 |     |                     cache.price,
 311 |     |                     cache.liquidity,
 312 |     |                     cache.amountLeft,
 313 |     |                     zeroForOne,
 314 |     |                     cache.exactIn
 315 |     |                 );
 316 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 317 |     |                     amountIn = cache.amountLeft;
 318 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, newPrice, uint256(cache.price), false);
 319 |     |                 } else {
 320 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, newPrice, uint256(cache.price), true);
 321 |     |                     amountOut = cache.amountLeft;
 322 |     |                 }
 323 |     |                 cache.amountLeft = 0;
 324 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 325 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(newPrice);
 326 |     |             } else {
 327 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 328 |     |                     amountIn = amountMax;
 329 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, false);
 330 |     | 
 331 |     |                 } else {
 332 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, true);
 333 |     |                     amountOut = amountMax;
 334 |     |                 }
 335 |     |                 cache.amountLeft -= amountMax;
 336 |     |                 if (nextPrice == cache.crossPrice) cache.cross = true;
 337 |     |                 else cache.cross = false;
 338 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(nextPrice);
 339 |     |             }
 340 |     |         } else {
 341 |     |             // Price is increasing.
 342 |     |             if (nextPrice > priceLimit) {
 343 |     |                 nextPrice = priceLimit;
 344 |     |             }
 345 |     |             uint256 amountMax = cache.exactIn ? ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, uint256(cache.price), nextPrice, true)
 346 |     |                                               : ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, uint256(cache.price), nextPrice, false);
 347 |     |             if (cache.amountLeft < amountMax) {
 348 |     |                 uint256 newPrice = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(
 349 |     |                     cache.price,
 350 |     |                     cache.liquidity,
 351 |     |                     cache.amountLeft,
 352 |     |                     zeroForOne,
 353 |     |                     cache.exactIn
 354 |     |                 );
 355 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 356 |     |                     amountIn = cache.amountLeft;
 357 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, cache.price, newPrice, false);
 358 |     |                 } else {
 359 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, cache.price, newPrice, true);
 360 |     |                     amountOut = cache.amountLeft;
 361 |     |                 }
 362 |     |                 cache.amountLeft = 0;
 363 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 364 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(newPrice);
 365 |     |             } else {
 366 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 367 |     |                     amountIn = amountMax;
 368 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, cache.price, nextPrice, false);
 369 |     |                 } else {
 370 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, cache.price, nextPrice, true);
 371 |     |                     amountOut = amountMax;
 372 |     |                 }
 373 |     |                 cache.amountLeft -= amountMax;
 374 |     |                 if (nextPrice == cache.crossPrice) cache.cross = true;
 375 |     |                 else cache.cross = false;
 376 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(nextPrice);
 377 |     |             }
 378 |     |         }
 379 |     |         cache = FeeMath.calculate(cache, amountIn, amountOut, zeroForOne);
 380 |     |         return cache;
 381 |     |     }
 382 |     | 
 383 |     |     function _cross(
 384 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 385 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 386 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 387 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 388 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams memory params
 389 |     |     ) internal returns (
 390 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 391 |     |     ) {
 392 |     | 
 393 |     |         // crossing range ticks
 394 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & RANGE_TICK) > 0) {
 395 |     |             if (!params.zeroForOne || (cache.amountLeft > 0 && params.priceLimit < cache.crossPrice)) {
 396 |     |                 PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory crossTick = ticks[cache.crossTick].range;
 397 |     |                 crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0       = cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0 - crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0;
 398 |     |                 crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1       = cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1 - crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1;
 399 |     |                 crossTick.tickSecondsAccumOutside = cache.tickSecondsAccum - crossTick.tickSecondsAccumOutside;
 400 |     |                 crossTick.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside = cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum - crossTick.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside;
 401 |     |                 ticks[cache.crossTick].range = crossTick;
 402 |     |                 int128 liquidityDelta = crossTick.liquidityDelta;
 403 |     |                 emit SyncRangeTick(
 404 |     |                     crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0,
 405 |     |                     crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1,
 406 |     |                     cache.crossTick
 407 |     |                 );
 408 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 409 |     |                     unchecked {
 410 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0){
 411 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-1");
 412 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(liquidityDelta);
 413 |     |                         } else {
 414 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-2");
 415 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(-liquidityDelta); 
 416 |     |                         }
 417 |     |                     }
 418 |     |                 } else {
 419 |     |                     unchecked {
 420 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0) {
 421 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-3");
 422 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 423 |     |                         } else {
 424 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-4");
 425 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 426 |     |                         }
 427 |     |                     }
 428 |     |                 }
 429 |     |             } else {
 430 |     |                 // if zeroForOne && amountLeft == 0 skip crossing the tick
 431 |     |                 /// @dev - this is so users can safely add liquidity with lower or upper at the pool price 
 432 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 433 |     |             }
 434 |     |             /// @dev - price and tickAtPrice updated at end of loop
 435 |     |         }
 436 |     |         // crossing limit tick
 437 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_TICK) > 0) {
 438 |     |             // cross limit tick
 439 |     |             EpochMap.set(cache.crossTick, !params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, limitTickMap, cache.constants);
 440 |     |             int128 liquidityDelta = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.liquidityDelta;
 441 |     | 
 442 |     |             if (liquidityDelta >= 0) {
 443 |     |                 cache.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 444 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) cache.state.pool1.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 445 |     |                 else cache.state.pool0.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 446 |     |             }
 447 |     |             else {
 448 |     |                 cache.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 449 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) cache.state.pool1.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 450 |     |                 else cache.state.pool0.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 451 |     |             }
 452 |     |             // zero out liquidityDelta and priceAt
 453 |     |             ticks[cache.crossTick].limit = PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick(0,0,0);
 454 |     |             LimitTicks.clear(ticks, cache.constants, limitTickMap, cache.crossTick);
 455 |     |             /// @dev - price and tickAtPrice updated at end of loop
 456 |     |         }
 457 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_POOL) > 0) {
 458 |     |             // add limit pool
 459 |     |             uint128 liquidityDelta = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool1.liquidity
 460 |     |                                                     : cache.state.pool0.liquidity;
 461 |     | 
 462 |     |             if (liquidityDelta > 0) cache.liquidity += liquidityDelta;
 463 |     |         }
 464 |     |         if (cache.cross)
 465 |     |             cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, false);
 466 |     | 
 467 |     |         return cache;
 468 |     |     }
 469 |     | 
 470 |     |     function _pass(
 471 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 472 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 473 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 474 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 475 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.QuoteParams memory params
 476 |     |     ) internal returns (
 477 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 478 |     |     ) {
 479 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & RANGE_TICK) > 0) {
 480 |     |             if (!params.zeroForOne || cache.amountLeft > 0) {
 481 |     |                 int128 liquidityDelta = ticks[cache.crossTick].range.liquidityDelta;
 482 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 483 |     |                     unchecked {
 484 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0){
 485 |     |                             // start of position boundary
 486 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-1");
 487 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(liquidityDelta);
 488 |     |                         } else {
 489 |     |                             // end of position boundary
 490 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-2");
 491 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(-liquidityDelta); 
 492 |     |                         }
 493 |     |                     }
 494 |     |                 } else {
 495 |     |                     unchecked {
 496 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0) {
 497 |     |                             // start of position boundary
 498 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-3");
 499 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 500 |     |                         } else {
 501 |     |                             // end of position boundary
 502 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-4");
 503 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 504 |     |                         }
 505 |     |                     }
 506 |     |                 }
 507 |     |             } else {
 508 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 509 |     |             }
 510 |     |         }
 511 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_TICK) > 0) {
 512 |     |             // cross limit tick
 513 |     |             int128 liquidityDelta = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.liquidityDelta;
 514 |     | 
 515 |     |             if (liquidityDelta > 0) {
 516 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 517 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool1.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-5");
 518 |     |                     cache.state.pool1.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 519 |     |                 } else {
 520 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool0.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-6");
 521 |     |                     cache.state.pool0.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 522 |     |                 }
 523 |     |             } 
 524 |     |             else {
 525 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 526 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool1.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-7");
 527 |     |                     cache.state.pool1.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 528 |     |                 } else {
 529 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool0.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-8");
 530 |     |                     cache.state.pool0.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 531 |     |                 }
 532 |     |             }
 533 |     |         }
 534 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_POOL) > 0) {
 535 |     |             // add limit pool
 536 |     |             uint128 liquidityDelta = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool1.liquidity
 537 |     |                                                     : cache.state.pool0.liquidity;
 538 |     | 
 539 |     |             if (liquidityDelta > 0) {
 540 |     |                 cache.liquidity += liquidityDelta;
 541 |     |             }
 542 |     |         }
 543 |     | 
 544 |     |         if (cache.cross)
 545 |     |             cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, false);
 546 |     | 
 547 |     |         return cache;
 548 |     |     }
 549 |     | 
 550 |     |     function _iterate(
 551 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 552 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 553 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 554 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 555 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 556 |     |         bool inclusive
 557 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 558 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory 
 559 |     |     )    
 560 |     |     {
 561 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 562 |     |             if (cache.price > cache.state.pool1.price) {
 563 |     |                 // load range pool
 564 |     |                 cache.limitActive = false;
 565 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity;
 566 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 567 |     |                 // next range tick vs. limit pool price
 568 |     |                 cache.crossTick = TickMap.previous(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 569 |     |                 cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 570 |     |                 if (cache.state.pool1.price >= cache.crossPrice) {
 571 |     |                     // cross into limit pool
 572 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = LIMIT_POOL;
 573 |     |                     if (cache.state.pool1.price == cache.crossPrice)
 574 |     |                         // also cross range tick
 575 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= RANGE_TICK;
 576 |     |                     else {
 577 |     |                         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool1.tickAtPrice;
 578 |     |                         cache.crossPrice = cache.state.pool1.price;
 579 |     |                     }
 580 |     |                 }
 581 |     |                 else {
 582 |     |                     // cross only range tick
 583 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = RANGE_TICK;
 584 |     |                 }
 585 |     |             } else {
 586 |     |                 // load range and limit pools
 587 |     |                 cache.limitActive = true;
 588 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity + cache.state.pool1.liquidity;
 589 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 590 |     |                 int24 rangeTickAhead; int24 limitTickAhead;
 591 |     |                 if (cache.crossStatus == LIMIT_POOL &&
 592 |     |                         cache.crossTick % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 &&
 593 |     |                         TickMap.get(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing))
 594 |     |                 {
 595 |     |                     limitTickAhead = cache.crossTick;
 596 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = cache.crossTick - cache.constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 597 |     |                 } else {
 598 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = TickMap.previous(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 599 |     |                     limitTickAhead = TickMap.previous(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 600 |     |                 }
 601 |     |                 // next range tick vs. next limit tick
 602 |     |                 
 603 |     |                 if (rangeTickAhead >= limitTickAhead) {
 604 |     |                     cache.crossTick = rangeTickAhead;
 605 |     |                     // cross range tick
 606 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = RANGE_TICK;
 607 |     |                     if (rangeTickAhead == limitTickAhead)
 608 |     |                         // also cross limit tick
 609 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= LIMIT_TICK;
 610 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 611 |     |                 } else {
 612 |     |                     // only cross limit tick
 613 |     |                     cache.crossTick = limitTickAhead;
 614 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = LIMIT_TICK;
 615 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt == 0 ? ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants)
 616 |     |                                                                                  : ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt;
 617 |     |                 }
 618 |     |             }
 619 |     |         } else {
 620 |     |             if (cache.price < cache.state.pool0.price) {
 621 |     |                 // load range pool
 622 |     |                 cache.limitActive = false;
 623 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity;
 624 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 625 |     |                 // next range tick vs. limit pool price
 626 |     |                 cache.crossTick = TickMap.next(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 627 |     |                 cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 628 |     |                 if (cache.state.pool0.price <= cache.crossPrice) {
 629 |     |                     // cross into limit pool
 630 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = LIMIT_POOL;
 631 |     |                     if (cache.state.pool0.price == cache.crossPrice)
 632 |     |                         // also cross range tick
 633 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= RANGE_TICK;
 634 |     |                     else {
 635 |     |                         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool0.tickAtPrice;
 636 |     |                         cache.crossPrice = cache.state.pool0.price;
 637 |     |                     }
 638 |     |                 }
 639 |     |                 else {
 640 |     |                     // cross only range tick
 641 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = RANGE_TICK;
 642 |     |                 }
 643 |     |             } else {
 644 |     |                 // load range and limit pools
 645 |     |                 cache.limitActive = true;
 646 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity + cache.state.pool0.liquidity;
 647 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 648 |     |                 // next range tick vs. next limit tick
 649 |     |                 int24 rangeTickAhead; int24 limitTickAhead;
 650 |     |                 if (cache.crossStatus == LIMIT_POOL &&
 651 |     |                         cache.crossTick % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 &&
 652 |     |                         TickMap.get(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing))
 653 |     |                 {
 654 |     |                     limitTickAhead = cache.crossTick;
 655 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = cache.crossTick + cache.constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 656 |     |                 } else {
 657 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = TickMap.next(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 658 |     |                     limitTickAhead = TickMap.next(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 659 |     |                 }
 660 |     |                 if (rangeTickAhead <= limitTickAhead) {
 661 |     |                     cache.crossTick = rangeTickAhead;
 662 |     |                     // cross range tick
 663 |     |                     cache.crossStatus |= RANGE_TICK;
 664 |     |                     if (rangeTickAhead == limitTickAhead)
 665 |     |                         // also cross limit tick
 666 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= LIMIT_TICK;
 667 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 668 |     |                 } else {
 669 |     |                     // only cross limit tick
 670 |     |                     cache.crossTick = limitTickAhead;
 671 |     |                     cache.crossStatus |= LIMIT_TICK;
 672 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt == 0 ? ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants)
 673 |     |                                                                                  : ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt;
 674 |     |                 }
 675 |     |             }
 676 |     |         }
 677 |     |         return cache;
 678 |     |     }
 679 |     | }
