   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import './EpochMap.sol';
   6 |     | import '../TickMap.sol';
   7 |     | import '../utils/String.sol';
   8 |     | import '../utils/SafeCast.sol';
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | library Claims {
  11 |     | 
  12 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     function validate(
  15 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  16 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  17 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
  18 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
  19 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  20 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory,
  21 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
  22 |     |     ) {
  23 |     |         // validate position liquidity
  24 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > cache.position.liquidity) require (false, 'NotEnoughPositionLiquidity()');
  25 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
  26 |     |             require(false, 'NoPositionLiquidityFound()');
  27 |     |         }
  28 |     |         
  29 |     |         if (params.claim < cache.position.lower ||
  30 |     |                 params.claim > cache.position.upper)
  31 |     |             require (false, 'InvalidClaimTick()');
  32 |     | 
  33 |     |         uint32 claimTickEpoch = EpochMap.get(params.claim, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  34 |     | 
  35 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne){
  36 |     |             if (cache.pool.price >= cache.priceClaim) {
  37 |     |                 if (cache.pool.price <= cache.priceUpper) {
  38 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.pool.price;
  39 |     |                     params.claim = TickMap.roundBack(cache.pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, cache.priceClaim);
  40 |     |                     claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  41 |     |                 } else {
  42 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceUpper;
  43 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.upper;
  44 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.upper].limit;
  45 |     |                 }
  46 |     |                 claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  47 |     |             } else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0) {
  48 |     |                 if (cache.claimTick.priceAt == 0) {
  49 |     |                     require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt1()');
  50 |     |                 }
  51 |     |                 cache.priceClaim = cache.claimTick.priceAt;
  52 |     |             }
  53 |     |         } else {
  54 |     |             if (cache.pool.price <= cache.priceClaim) {
  55 |     |                 if (cache.pool.price >= cache.priceLower) {
  56 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.pool.price;
  57 |     |                     params.claim = TickMap.roundBack(cache.pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, cache.priceClaim);
  58 |     |                     claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  59 |     |                 } else {
  60 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceLower;
  61 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.lower;
  62 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.upper].limit;
  63 |     | 
  64 |     |                 }
  65 |     |                 claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  66 |     |             } else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0) {
  67 |     |                 if (cache.claimTick.priceAt == 0) {
  68 |     |                     require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt2()');
  69 |     |                 }
  70 |     |                 cache.priceClaim = cache.claimTick.priceAt;
  71 |     |             }
  72 |     |         }
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |         // validate claim tick
  75 |     |         if (params.claim == (params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : cache.position.lower)) {
  76 |     |             // set params.amount to 0 for event emitted at end
  77 |     |             cache.liquidityBurned = 0;
  78 |     |              if (claimTickEpoch <= cache.position.epochLast)
  79 |     |                 require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt3()');
  80 |     |         } else if (cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
  81 |     |             /// @dev - partway claim is valid as long as liquidity is not being removed
  82 |     | 
  83 |     |             // if we cleared the final tick of their position, this is the wrong claim tick
  84 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
  85 |     |                 uint32 endTickEpoch = EpochMap.get(cache.position.upper, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  86 |     |                 if (endTickEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
  87 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.upper;
  88 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceUpper;
  89 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.upper].limit;
  90 |     |                     cache.liquidityBurned = cache.position.liquidity;
  91 |     |                 } else {
  92 |     |                     int24 claimTickNext = TickMap.next(tickMap, params.claim, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  93 |     |                     uint32 claimTickNextEpoch = EpochMap.get(claimTickNext, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  94 |     |                     ///@dev - next swapEpoch should not be greater
  95 |     |                     if (claimTickNextEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
  96 |     |                         require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt5()');
  97 |     |                     }
  98 |     |                 }
  99 |     |             } else {
 100 |     |                 uint32 endTickEpoch = EpochMap.get(cache.position.lower, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
 101 |     |                 if (endTickEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
 102 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.lower;
 103 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceLower;
 104 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.lower].limit;
 105 |     |                     cache.liquidityBurned = cache.position.liquidity;
 106 |     |                 } else {
 107 |     |                     int24 claimTickNext = TickMap.previous(tickMap, params.claim, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
 108 |     |                     uint32 claimTickNextEpoch = EpochMap.get(claimTickNext, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
 109 |     |                     ///@dev - next swapEpoch should not be greater
 110 |     |                     if (claimTickNextEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
 111 |     |                         require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt5()');
 112 |     |                     }
 113 |     |                 }
 114 |     |             }
 115 |     |         }
 116 |     |         /// @dev - start tick does not overwrite position and final tick clears position
 117 |     |         if (params.claim != cache.position.upper && params.claim != cache.position.lower) {
 118 |     |             // check epochLast on claim tick
 119 |     |             if (claimTickEpoch <= cache.position.epochLast)
 120 |     |                 require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt7()');
 121 |     |         }
 122 |     | 
 123 |     |         // early return if no update and amount burned is 0
 124 |     |         //TODO: after we've cycled through claim ticks and there are no position updates just revert - DONE
 125 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim == cache.position.lower
 126 |     |                               : params.claim == cache.position.upper) {
 127 |     |             if (cache.liquidityBurned == 0)
 128 |     |                 require(false, 'NoPositionUpdates()');
 129 |     |         }
 130 |     | 
 131 |     |         return (params, cache);
 132 |     |     }
 133 |     | 
 134 |     |     function getDeltas(
 135 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
 136 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 137 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 138 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 139 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 140 |     |     ) {
 141 |     |         // if half tick priceAt > 0 add amountOut to amountOutClaimed
 142 |     |         // set claimPriceLast if zero
 143 |     |         if (!cache.position.crossedInto) {
 144 |     |             cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 145 |     |         }
 146 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.GetDeltasLocals memory locals;
 147 |     | 
 148 |     |         if (params.claim % constants.tickSpacing != 0)
 149 |     |         // this should pass price at the claim tick
 150 |     |             locals.previousFullTick = TickMap.roundBack(params.claim, constants, params.zeroForOne, ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.claim, constants));
 151 |     |         else
 152 |     |             locals.previousFullTick = params.claim;
 153 |     |         locals.pricePrevious = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(locals.previousFullTick, constants);
 154 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? locals.previousFullTick > cache.position.lower
 155 |     |                               : locals.previousFullTick < cache.position.upper) {
 156 |     |             
 157 |     |             // claim amounts up to latest full tick crossed
 158 |     |             cache.amountIn += uint128(params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.position.liquidity, cache.priceLower, locals.pricePrevious, false)
 159 |     |                                                                  : ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.position.liquidity, locals.pricePrevious, cache.priceUpper, false));
 160 |     |         }
 161 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
 162 |     |            // if tick hasn't been set back calculate amountIn
 163 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceClaim > locals.pricePrevious
 164 |     |                                   : cache.priceClaim < locals.pricePrevious) {
 165 |     |                 // allow partial tick claim if removing liquidity
 166 |     |                 cache.amountIn += uint128(params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidityBurned, locals.pricePrevious, cache.priceClaim, false)
 167 |     |                                                             : ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidityBurned, cache.priceClaim, locals.pricePrevious, false));
 168 |     |             }
 169 |     |             // use priceClaim if tick hasn't been set back
 170 |     |             // else use claimPriceLast to calculate amountOut
 171 |     |             if (params.claim != (params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : cache.position.lower)) {
 172 |     |                 cache.amountOut += uint128(params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidityBurned, cache.priceClaim, cache.priceUpper, false)
 173 |     |                                                              : ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidityBurned, cache.priceLower, cache.priceClaim, false));
 174 |     |             }
 175 |     |         }
 176 |     |         // take protocol fee if needed
 177 |     |         if (cache.pool.protocolFillFee > 0 && cache.amountIn > 0) {
 178 |     |             uint128 protocolFeeAmount = OverflowMath.mulDiv(cache.amountIn, cache.pool.protocolFillFee, 1e4).toUint128();
 179 |     |             cache.amountIn -= protocolFeeAmount;
 180 |     |             cache.pool.protocolFees += protocolFeeAmount;
 181 |     |         }
 182 |     |         return cache;
 183 |     |     }
 184 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/limit/EpochMap.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../math/ConstantProduct.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   6 |     | 
   7 |     | library EpochMap {
   8 |     |     event SyncLimitTick(
   9 |     |         uint32 epoch,
  10 |     |         int24 tick,
  11 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  12 |     |     );
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     function set(
  15 |     |         int24  tick,
  16 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  17 |     |         uint256 epoch,
  18 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  19 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
  20 |     |     ) internal {
  21 |     |         (
  22 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  23 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  24 |     |             uint256 blockIndex,
  25 |     |             uint256 volumeIndex
  26 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, constants);
  27 |     |         // assert epoch isn't bigger than max uint32
  28 |     |         uint256 epochValue = zeroForOne ? tickMap.epochs0[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex]
  29 |     |                                         : tickMap.epochs1[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex];
  30 |     |         // clear previous value
  31 |     |         epochValue &=  ~(((1 << 9) - 1) << ((tickIndex & 0x7) * 32));
  32 |     |         // add new value to word
  33 |     |         epochValue |= epoch << ((tickIndex & 0x7) * 32);
  34 |     |         // store word in map
  35 |     |         zeroForOne ? tickMap.epochs0[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex] = epochValue
  36 |     |                    : tickMap.epochs1[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex] = epochValue;
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |         emit SyncLimitTick(uint32(epoch), tick, zeroForOne);
  39 |     |     }
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |     function get(
  42 |     |         int24 tick,
  43 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  44 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  45 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
  46 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  47 |     |         uint32 epoch
  48 |     |     ) {
  49 |     |         (
  50 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  51 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  52 |     |             uint256 blockIndex,
  53 |     |             uint256 volumeIndex
  54 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, constants);
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |         uint256 epochValue = zeroForOne ? tickMap.epochs0[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex]
  57 |     |                                         : tickMap.epochs1[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex];
  58 |     |         // right shift so first 8 bits are epoch value
  59 |     |         epochValue >>= ((tickIndex & 0x7) * 32);
  60 |     |         // clear other bits
  61 |     |         epochValue &= ((1 << 32) - 1);
  62 |     |         return uint32(epochValue);
  63 |     |     }
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |     function getIndices(
  66 |     |         int24 tick,
  67 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
  68 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
  69 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  70 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  71 |     |             uint256 blockIndex,
  72 |     |             uint256 volumeIndex
  73 |     |         )
  74 |     |     {
  75 |     |         unchecked {
  76 |     |             if (tick > ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing)) require (false, 'TickIndexOverflow()');
  77 |     |             if (tick < ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing)) require (false, 'TickIndexUnderflow()');
  78 |     |             if (tick % (constants.tickSpacing / 2) != 0) {
  79 |     |                 require (false, 'TickIndexInvalid()');
  80 |     |             } 
  81 |     |             tickIndex = uint256(int256((_round(tick, constants.tickSpacing / 2) 
  82 |     |                                         - _round(ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK, constants.tickSpacing / 2)) 
  83 |     |                                         / (constants.tickSpacing / 2)));
  84 |     |             wordIndex = tickIndex >> 3;        // 2^3 epochs per word
  85 |     |             blockIndex = tickIndex >> 11;      // 2^8 words per block
  86 |     |             volumeIndex = tickIndex >> 19;     // 2^8 blocks per volume
  87 |     |             if (blockIndex > 2046) require (false, 'BlockIndexOverflow()');
  88 |     |         }
  89 |     |     }
  90 |     | 
  91 |     |     function _round(
  92 |     |         int24 tick,
  93 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  94 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
  95 |     |         int24 roundedTick
  96 |     |     ) {
  97 |     |         return tick / tickSpacing * tickSpacing;
  98 |     |     }
  99 |     | }

  15 |     | /// @notice Position management library for ranged liquidity.
  16 |     | /// @notice Position management library for ranged liquidity.
  17 |     | library LimitPositions {
  18 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  19 |     | 
  20 |     |     event BurnLimit(
  21 |     |         address indexed to,
  22 |     |         uint32 positionId,

  24 |     |         int24 upper,
  25 |     |         int24 oldClaim,

  28 |     |         uint128 liquidityBurned,
  29 |     |         uint128 tokenInClaimed,

  32 |     | 
  33 |     |     function resize(
  34 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  35 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  36 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  37 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  38 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
  39 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
  40 |     |     ) internal returns (
  41 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory,
  42 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory
  43 |     |     )
  44 |     |     {
  45 |     |         ConstantProduct.checkTicks(params.lower, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing);
  46 |     | 
  47 |     |         cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
  48 |     |         cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
  49 |     |         cache.mintSize = uint256(params.mintPercent) * uint256(params.amount) / 1e28;
  50 |     | 
  51 |     |         // calculate L constant
  52 |     |         cache.liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
  53 |     |             cache.priceLower,
  54 |     |             cache.priceUpper,
  55 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower : cache.priceUpper,
  56 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? 0 : uint256(params.amount),
  57 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? uint256(params.amount) : 0
  58 |     |         );
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0) require (false, 'PositionLiquidityZero()');
  61 |     |         // calculate price limit by using half of input
  62 |     |         {
  63 |     |             cache.priceLimit = params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(cache.priceUpper, cache.liquidityMinted, params.amount / 2, true, true)
  64 |     |                                                  : ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(cache.priceLower, cache.liquidityMinted, params.amount / 2, false, true);
  65 |     |             if (cache.priceLimit == 0) require (false, 'PriceLimitZero()');
  66 |     |             // get tick at price
  67 |     |             cache.tickLimit = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(cache.priceLimit.toUint160(), cache.constants);
  68 |     |             // round to nearest tick spacing
  69 |     |             cache.priceLimit = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.tickLimit, cache.constants);
  70 |     |         }
  71 |     | 
  72 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory swapCache;
  73 |     |         swapCache.state = cache.state;
  74 |     |         swapCache.constants = cache.constants;
  75 |     |         swapCache.price = cache.state.pool.price;
  76 |     | 
  77 |     |         // swap zero if no liquidity near market price
  78 |     |         if (cache.state.pool.liquidity == 0 && 
  79 |     |             (params.zeroForOne ? swapCache.price > cache.priceLower
  80 |     |                                : swapCache.price < cache.priceUpper)) {
  81 |     |             swapCache = Ticks.swap(
  82 |     |                 ticks,
  83 |     |                 samples,
  84 |     |                 rangeTickMap,
  85 |     |                 limitTickMap,
  86 |     |                 PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams({
  87 |     |                     to: params.to,
  88 |     |                     priceLimit: (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower 
  89 |     |                                                    : cache.priceUpper).toUint160(),
  90 |     |                     amount: 0,
  91 |     |                     //TODO: handle exactOut
  92 |     |                     exactIn: true,
  93 |     |                     zeroForOne: params.zeroForOne,
  94 |     |                     callbackData: abi.encodePacked(bytes1(0x0))
  95 |     |                 }),
  96 |     |                 swapCache
  97 |     |             );
  98 |     |         }
  99 |     | 
 100 |     |         // only swap if priceLimit is beyond current pool price
 101 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLimit < swapCache.price
 102 |     |                               : cache.priceLimit > swapCache.price) {
 103 |     |             // swap and save the pool state
 104 |     |             swapCache = Ticks.swap(
 105 |     |                 ticks,
 106 |     |                 samples,
 107 |     |                 rangeTickMap,
 108 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 109 |     |                 PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams({
 110 |     |                     to: params.to,
 111 |     |                     priceLimit: cache.priceLimit.toUint160(),
 112 |     |                     amount: params.amount,
 113 |     |                     //TODO: handle exactOut
 114 |     |                     exactIn: true,
 115 |     |                     zeroForOne: params.zeroForOne,
 116 |     |                     callbackData: abi.encodePacked(bytes1(0x0))
 117 |     |                 }),
 118 |     |                 swapCache
 119 |     |             );
 120 |     |             // subtract from remaining input amount
 121 |     |             params.amount -= uint128(swapCache.input);
 122 |     | 
 123 |     |         }
 124 |     |         // save to cache
 125 |     |         cache.swapCache = swapCache;
 126 |     |         cache.state = swapCache.state;
 127 |     | 
 128 |     |         if (params.amount < cache.mintSize) params.amount = 0;
 129 |     |         // move start tick based on amount filled in swap
 130 |     |         if ((params.amount > 0 && swapCache.input > 0) ||
 131 |     |             (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower < swapCache.price
 132 |     |                                : cache.priceUpper > swapCache.price)
 133 |     |         ) {
 134 |     |             // move the tick limit based on pool.tickAtPrice
 135 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower < swapCache.price
 136 |     |                                   : cache.priceUpper > swapCache.price) {
 137 |     |                 cache.tickLimit = swapCache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 138 |     |             }
 139 |     |             // round ahead tickLimit to avoid crossing epochs
 140 |     |             cache.tickLimit = TickMap.roundAhead(cache.tickLimit, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, swapCache.price);
 141 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 142 |     |                 if (cache.priceLower < swapCache.price) {
 143 |     |                     // if rounding goes past limit trim position
 144 |     |                     /// @dev - if swap didn't go to limit user would be 100% filled
 145 |     |                     params.lower = cache.tickLimit;
 146 |     |                     cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 147 |     |                 }
 148 |     |                 if (params.lower >= params.upper && 
 149 |     |                     params.lower < ConstantProduct.maxTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing) - cache.constants.tickSpacing
 150 |     |                 ) {
 151 |     |                     params.upper = params.lower + cache.constants.tickSpacing;
 152 |     |                 }
 153 |     |                 cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 154 |     |             } else {
 155 |     |                 if (cache.priceUpper > swapCache.price) {
 156 |     |                     // if rounding goes past limit trim position
 157 |     |                     params.upper = cache.tickLimit;
 158 |     |                     cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 159 |     |                 }
 160 |     |                 if (params.upper <= params.lower && 
 161 |     |                     params.lower > ConstantProduct.minTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing) + cache.constants.tickSpacing
 162 |     |                 ) {
 163 |     |                     params.lower = params.upper - cache.constants.tickSpacing;
 164 |     |                 }
 165 |     |                 cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 166 |     |             }
 167 |     |             if (params.amount > 0 && params.lower < params.upper)
 168 |     |                 cache.liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
 169 |     |                     cache.priceLower,
 170 |     |                     cache.priceUpper,
 171 |     |                     params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower : cache.priceUpper,
 172 |     |                     params.zeroForOne ? 0 : uint256(params.amount),
 173 |     |                     params.zeroForOne ? uint256(params.amount) : 0
 174 |     |                 );
 175 |     |             else
 176 |     |                 /// @auditor unnecessary since params.amount is 0
 177 |     |                 cache.liquidityMinted = 0;
 178 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1;
 179 |     |         }
 180 |     | 
 181 |     |         /// @dev - for safety
 182 |     |         if (params.lower >= params.upper) {
 183 |     |             // zero out amount transferred in
 184 |     |             params.amount = 0;
 185 |     |         }
 186 |     | 
 187 |     |         return (
 188 |     |             params,
 189 |     |             cache
 190 |     |         );
 191 |     |     }
 192 |     | 
 193 |     |     function add(
 194 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 195 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 196 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 197 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params
 198 |     |     ) internal returns (
 199 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory,
 200 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition memory
 201 |     |     ) {
 202 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0) return (cache.pool, cache.position);
 203 |     | 
 204 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
 205 |     |             cache.position.epochLast = cache.state.epoch;
 206 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1; // increment for future swaps
 207 |     |             IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).mint(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
 208 |     |         } else {
 209 |     |             // safety check in case we somehow get here
 210 |     |             if (
 211 |     |                 params.zeroForOne
 212 |     |                     ? EpochMap.get(params.lower, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants)
 213 |     |                             > cache.position.epochLast
 214 |     |                     : EpochMap.get(params.upper, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants)
 215 |     |                             > cache.position.epochLast
 216 |     |             ) {
 217 |     |                 require (false, 'PositionAlreadyEntered()');
 218 |     |             }
 219 |     |             /// @auditor maybe this shouldn't be a revert but rather just not mint the position?
 220 |     |         }
 221 |     |         
 222 |     |         // add liquidity to ticks
 223 |     |         LimitTicks.insert(
 224 |     |             ticks,
 225 |     |             tickMap,
 226 |     |             cache,
 227 |     |             params
 228 |     |         );
 229 |     | 
 230 |     |         // update liquidity global
 231 |     |         cache.state.liquidityGlobal += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 232 |     | 
 233 |     |         cache.position.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 234 |     | 
 235 |     |         return (cache.pool, cache.position);
 236 |     |     }
 237 |     | 
 238 |     |     function update(
 239 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 240 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 241 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 242 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params
 243 |     |     ) internal returns (
 244 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory,
 245 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 246 |     |     )
 247 |     |     {
 248 |     |         (
 249 |     |             params,
 250 |     |             cache
 251 |     |         ) = _deltas(
 252 |     |             ticks,
 253 |     |             tickMap,
 254 |     |             params,
 255 |     |             cache
 256 |     |         );
 257 |     | 
 258 |     |         // update pool liquidity
 259 |     |         if (cache.priceClaim == cache.pool.price && cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
 260 |     |             // handle pool.price at edge of range
 261 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceClaim < cache.priceUpper
 262 |     |                                   : cache.priceClaim > cache.priceLower)
 263 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.pool.liquidity, cache.liquidityBurned, "PLU-3");
 264 |     |                 cache.pool.liquidity -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 265 |     |         }
 266 |     | 
 267 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
 268 |     |             if (params.claim == (params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : cache.position.lower)) {
 269 |     |                 // if claim is final tick no liquidity to remove
 270 |     |                 cache.removeLower = false;
 271 |     |                 cache.removeUpper = false;
 272 |     |             } else {
 273 |     |                 // else remove liquidity from final tick
 274 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.removeUpper = true 
 275 |     |                                   : cache.removeLower = true;
 276 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 277 |     | 
 278 |     |                     if (params.claim == cache.position.lower && 
 279 |     |                         cache.pool.price < cache.priceLower
 280 |     |                     ) {
 281 |     |                         // full tick price was touched
 282 |     |                         cache.removeLower = true;
 283 |     |                     } else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 && 
 284 |     |                                     cache.pool.price < cache.priceClaim)
 285 |     |                         // half tick was created
 286 |     |                         cache.removeLower = true;
 287 |     |                 } else {
 288 |     |                     if (params.claim == cache.position.upper &&
 289 |     |                         cache.pool.price > cache.priceUpper
 290 |     |                     )
 291 |     |                         // full tick price was touched
 292 |     |                         cache.removeUpper = true;
 293 |     |                     else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 &&
 294 |     |                                     cache.pool.price > cache.priceClaim)
 295 |     |                         // half tick was created
 296 |     |                         cache.removeUpper = true;
 297 |     |                 }
 298 |     |             }
 299 |     |             LimitTicks.remove(
 300 |     |                 ticks,
 301 |     |                 tickMap,
 302 |     |                 params,
 303 |     |                 cache,
 304 |     |                 cache.constants
 305 |     |             );
 306 |     |             // update position liquidity
 307 |     |             cache.position.liquidity -= uint128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 308 |     |             // update global liquidity
 309 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(cache.state.liquidityGlobal, cache.liquidityBurned, "LGU-2");
 310 |     |             cache.state.liquidityGlobal -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 311 |     |         }
 312 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim == cache.position.upper
 313 |     |                               : params.claim == cache.position.lower) {
 314 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(cache.state.liquidityGlobal, cache.position.liquidity, "LGU-3");
 315 |     |             cache.state.liquidityGlobal -= cache.position.liquidity;
 316 |     |             cache.position.liquidity = 0;
 317 |     |         }
 318 |     |         // clear out old position
 319 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim != cache.position.lower 
 320 |     |                               : params.claim != cache.position.upper) {
 321 |     |             /// @dev - this also clears out position end claims
 322 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim == cache.position.lower 
 323 |     |                                   : params.claim == cache.position.upper) {
 324 |     |                 // subtract remaining position liquidity out from global
 325 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(cache.state.liquidityGlobal, cache.position.liquidity, "LGU-4");
 326 |     |                 cache.state.liquidityGlobal -= cache.position.liquidity;
 327 |     |             }
 328 |     |         }
 329 |     |         // clear position if empty
 330 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
 331 |     |             cache.position.epochLast = 0;
 332 |     |             cache.position.crossedInto = false;
 333 |     |         }
 334 |     | 
 335 |     |         // round back claim tick for storage
 336 |     |         if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0) {
 337 |     |             cache.claim = params.claim;
 338 |     |             params.claim = TickMap.roundBack(params.claim, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, cache.priceClaim);
 339 |     |         }
 340 |     |         
 341 |     |         emit BurnLimit(
 342 |     |             params.to,
 343 |     |             params.positionId,
 344 |     |             cache.position.lower,
 345 |     |             cache.position.upper,
 346 |     |             cache.claim,
 347 |     |             params.claim,
 348 |     |             params.zeroForOne,
 349 |     |             cache.liquidityBurned,
 350 |     |             cache.amountIn,
 351 |     |             cache.amountOut
 352 |     |         );
 353 |     | 
 354 |     |         // save pool to state in memory
 355 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne) cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool;
 356 |     |         else cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 357 |     | 
 358 |     |         return (params, cache);
 359 |     |     }
 360 |     | 
 361 |     |     function snapshot(
 362 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 363 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 364 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 365 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params
 366 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 367 |     |         uint128 amountIn,
 368 |     |         uint128 amountOut
 369 |     |     ) {
 370 |     |         (
 371 |     |             params,
 372 |     |             cache
 373 |     |         ) = _deltas(
 374 |     |             ticks,
 375 |     |             tickMap,
 376 |     |             params,
 377 |     |             cache
 378 |     |         );
 379 |     | 
 380 |     |         return (cache.amountIn, cache.amountOut);
 381 |     |     }
 382 |     | 
 383 |     |     function _deltas(
 384 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 385 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 386 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
 387 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
 388 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 389 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory,
 390 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 391 |     |     ) {
 392 |     |         cache = LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache({
 393 |     |             state: cache.state,
 394 |     |             pool: params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1,
 395 |     |             claimTick: ticks[params.claim].limit,
 396 |     |             position: cache.position,
 397 |     |             constants: cache.constants,
 398 |     |             priceLower: ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.lower, cache.constants),
 399 |     |             priceClaim: ticks[params.claim].limit.priceAt == 0 ? ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.claim, cache.constants)
 400 |     |                                                                : ticks[params.claim].limit.priceAt,
 401 |     |             priceUpper: ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.upper, cache.constants),
 402 |     |             liquidityBurned: _convert(cache.position.liquidity, params.burnPercent),
 403 |     |             amountIn: 0,
 404 |     |             amountOut: 0,
 405 |     |             claim: params.claim,
 406 |     |             removeLower: false,
 407 |     |             removeUpper: false
 408 |     |         });
 409 |     | 
 410 |     |         // check claim is valid
 411 |     |         (params, cache) = Claims.validate(
 412 |     |             ticks,
 413 |     |             tickMap,
 414 |     |             params,
 415 |     |             cache
 416 |     |         );
 417 |     | 
 418 |     |         // calculate position deltas
 419 |     |         cache = Claims.getDeltas(params, cache, cache.constants);
 420 |     | 
 421 |     |         return (params, cache);
 422 |     |     }
 423 |     | 
 424 |     |     function _convert(
 425 |     |         uint128 liquidity,
 426 |     |         uint128 percent
 427 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 428 |     |         uint128
 429 |     |     ) {
 430 |     |         // convert percentage to liquidity amount
 431 |     |         if (percent > 1e38) percent = 1e38;
 432 |     |         if (liquidity == 0 && percent > 0) require (false, 'PositionNotFound()');
 433 |     |         return uint128(uint256(liquidity) * uint256(percent) / 1e38);
 434 |     |     }

  16 |     | /// @notice Tick management library for limit pools
  17 |     | library LimitTicks {
  18 |     |     error LiquidityOverflow();
  19 |     |     error LiquidityUnderflow();
  20 |     |     error InvalidLowerTick();
  21 |     |     error InvalidUpperTick();
  22 |     |     error InvalidPositionAmount();
  23 |     |     error InvalidPositionBounds();
  24 |     | 
  25 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  26 |     | 
  27 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q96 = 0x1000000000000000000000000;
  28 |     | 
  29 |     |     event SyncLimitLiquidity(
  30 |     |         uint128 liquidityAdded,
  31 |     |         int24 tick,
  32 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  33 |     |     );
  34 |     | 
  35 |     |     function validate(
  36 |     |         int24 lower,
  37 |     |         int24 upper,
  38 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  39 |     |     ) internal pure {
  40 |     |         if (lower % tickSpacing != 0) require(false, 'InvalidLowerTick()');
  41 |     |         if (lower <= ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK) require(false, 'InvalidLowerTick()');
  42 |     |         if (upper % tickSpacing != 0) require(false, 'InvalidUpperTick()');
  43 |     |         if (upper >= ConstantProduct.MAX_TICK) require(false, 'InvalidUpperTick()');
  44 |     |         if (lower >= upper) require(false, 'InvalidPositionBounds()');
  45 |     |     }
  46 |     | 
  47 |     |     function insert(
  48 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  49 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  50 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
  51 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params
  52 |     |     ) internal {
  53 |     |         /// @auditor - validation of ticks is in Positions.validate
  54 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted > (uint128(type(int128).max) - cache.state.liquidityGlobal) )
  55 |     |             require (false, 'LiquidityOverflow()');
  56 |     | 
  57 |     |         int256 liquidityMinted = int256(cache.liquidityMinted);
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |         // check if adding liquidity necessary
  60 |     |         if (!params.zeroForOne || cache.priceLower > cache.pool.price) {
  61 |     |             // sets bit in map
  62 |     |             if(!TickMap.set(tickMap, params.lower, cache.constants.tickSpacing)){
  63 |     |                 // inherit epoch 
  64 |     |                 int24 tickAhead;
  65 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  66 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.next(tickMap, params.lower, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  67 |     |                 } else {
  68 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.previous(tickMap, params.lower, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  69 |     |                 }
  70 |     |                 uint32 epochAhead = EpochMap.get(tickAhead, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  71 |     |                 EpochMap.set(params.lower, params.zeroForOne, epochAhead, tickMap, cache.constants);
  72 |     |             }
  73 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickLower = ticks[params.lower].limit;
  74 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
  75 |     |                 tickLower.liquidityDelta += int128(liquidityMinted);
  76 |     |             } else {
  77 |     |                 tickLower.liquidityDelta -= int128(liquidityMinted);
  78 |     |             }
  79 |     |             tickLower.liquidityAbsolute += cache.liquidityMinted.toUint128();
  80 |     |             ticks[params.lower].limit = tickLower;
  81 |     |         } else {
  82 |     |             /// @dev - i.e. if zeroForOne && cache.priceLower <= cache.pool.price
  83 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1;
  84 |     |             // mark epoch on undercut tick
  85 |     |             EpochMap.set(params.lower, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
  86 |     |         }
  87 |     | 
  88 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne || cache.priceUpper < cache.pool.price) {
  89 |     |             if(!TickMap.set(tickMap, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing)) {
  90 |     |                 int24 tickAhead;
  91 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  92 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.next(tickMap, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  93 |     |                 } else {
  94 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.previous(tickMap, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  95 |     |                 }
  96 |     |                 uint32 epochAhead = EpochMap.get(tickAhead, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  97 |     |                 EpochMap.set(params.upper, params.zeroForOne, epochAhead, tickMap, cache.constants);
  98 |     |             }
  99 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickUpper = ticks[params.upper].limit;
 100 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 101 |     |                 tickUpper.liquidityDelta -= int128(liquidityMinted);
 102 |     |             } else {
 103 |     |                 tickUpper.liquidityDelta += int128(liquidityMinted);
 104 |     |             }
 105 |     |             tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute += cache.liquidityMinted.toUint128();
 106 |     |             ticks[params.upper].limit = tickUpper;
 107 |     |         } else {
 108 |     |             /// @dev - i.e. if !zeroForOne && cache.priceUpper >= cache.pool.price
 109 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1;
 110 |     |             // mark epoch on undercut tick
 111 |     |             EpochMap.set(params.upper, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
 112 |     |         }
 113 |     |     }
 114 |     | 
 115 |     |     function insertSingle(
 116 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
 117 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 118 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 119 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 120 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool,
 121 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 122 |     |     ) internal returns (
 123 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory
 124 |     |     ){
 125 |     |         /// @auditor - would be smart to protect against the case of epochs crossing
 126 |     |         (
 127 |     |             int24 tickToSave,
 128 |     |             uint160 roundedPrice
 129 |     |         ) = TickMap.roundHalf(pool.tickAtPrice, constants, pool.price);
 130 |     |         // update tick to save
 131 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.LimitTick memory tick = ticks[tickToSave].limit;
 132 |     |         /// @auditor - tick.priceAt will be zero for tick % tickSpacing == 0
 133 |     |         if (tick.priceAt == 0) {
 134 |     |             if (pool.price != (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower : cache.priceUpper)) {
 135 |     |                 TickMap.set(tickMap, tickToSave, constants.tickSpacing);
 136 |     |             }
 137 |     |             EpochMap.set(tickToSave, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, constants);
 138 |     |         }
 139 |     |         // skip if we are at the nearest full tick
 140 |     |         if(pool.price != roundedPrice) {
 141 |     |             // if empty just save the pool price
 142 |     |             if (tick.priceAt == 0) {
 143 |     |                 tick.priceAt = pool.price;
 144 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertTickAtPriceDivisibleByTickSpacing(tickToSave, ticks[tickToSave].limit.priceAt, constants.tickSpacing);
 145 |     |             }
 146 |     |             else {
 147 |     |                 // we need to blend the two partial fills into a single tick
 148 |     |                 LimitPoolStructs.InsertSingleLocals memory locals;
 149 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 150 |     |                     // 0 -> 1 positions price moves up so nextFullTick is greater
 151 |     |                     locals.previousFullTick = tickToSave - constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 152 |     |                     locals.pricePrevious = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(locals.previousFullTick, constants);
 153 |     |                     // calculate amountOut filled across both partial fills
 154 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact = ConstantProduct.getDy(pool.liquidity, locals.pricePrevious, pool.price, false);
 155 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact += ConstantProduct.getDy(uint128(tick.liquidityDelta), locals.pricePrevious, tick.priceAt, false);
 156 |     |                     // add current pool liquidity to partial tick
 157 |     |                     uint128 combinedLiquidity = pool.liquidity + uint128(tick.liquidityDelta);
 158 |     |                     // advance price based on combined fill
 159 |     |                     tick.priceAt = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(uint256(locals.pricePrevious), combinedLiquidity, locals.amountOutExact, false, true).toUint160();
 160 |     |                     // dx to the next tick is less than before the tick blend
 161 |     |                     EpochMap.set(tickToSave, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, constants);
 162 |     |                 } else {
 163 |     |                     // 0 -> 1 positions price moves up so nextFullTick is lesser
 164 |     |                     locals.previousFullTick = tickToSave + constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 165 |     |                     locals.pricePrevious = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(locals.previousFullTick, constants);
 166 |     |                     // calculate amountOut filled across both partial fills
 167 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact = ConstantProduct.getDx(pool.liquidity, pool.price, locals.pricePrevious, false);
 168 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact += ConstantProduct.getDx(uint128(tick.liquidityDelta), tick.priceAt, locals.pricePrevious, false);
 169 |     |                     // add current pool liquidity to partial tick
 170 |     |                     uint128 combinedLiquidity = pool.liquidity + uint128(tick.liquidityDelta);
 171 |     |                     // advance price based on combined fill
 172 |     |                     tick.priceAt = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(uint256(locals.pricePrevious), combinedLiquidity, locals.amountOutExact, true, true).toUint160();
 173 |     |                     // mark epoch for second partial fill positions
 174 |     |                     EpochMap.set(tickToSave, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, constants);
 175 |     |                 }
 176 |     |             }
 177 |     |         }
 178 |     |         // invariant => if we save liquidity to tick clear pool liquidity
 179 |     |         if ((tickToSave != (params.zeroForOne ? params.lower : params.upper))) {
 180 |     |             tick.liquidityDelta += int128(pool.liquidity);
 181 |     |             tick.liquidityAbsolute += pool.liquidity;
 182 |     |             emit SyncLimitLiquidity(pool.liquidity, tickToSave, params.zeroForOne);
 183 |     |             pool.liquidity = 0;
 184 |     |         }
 185 |     |         ticks[tickToSave].limit = tick;
 186 |     |         return pool;
 187 |     |     }
 188 |     | 
 189 |     |     function remove(
 190 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 191 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 192 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
 193 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 194 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 195 |     |     ) internal {
 196 |     |         // set ticks based on claim and zeroForOne
 197 |     |         int24 lower = params.zeroForOne ? params.claim : cache.position.lower;
 198 |     |         int24 upper = params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : params.claim;
 199 |     |         {    
 200 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickLower = ticks[lower].limit;
 201 |     |             
 202 |     |             if (cache.removeLower) {
 203 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 204 |     |                     tickLower.liquidityDelta -= int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 205 |     |                 } else {
 206 |     |                     tickLower.liquidityDelta += int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 207 |     |                 }
 208 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityAbsoluteUnderflows(tickLower.liquidityAbsolute, cache.liquidityBurned, 'TSL-1');
 209 |     |                 tickLower.liquidityAbsolute -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 210 |     |                 ticks[lower].limit = tickLower;
 211 |     |                 clear(ticks, constants, tickMap, lower);
 212 |     |             }
 213 |     |         }
 214 |     |         {
 215 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickUpper = ticks[upper].limit;
 216 |     |             if (cache.removeUpper) {
 217 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 218 |     |                     tickUpper.liquidityDelta += int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 219 |     |                 } else {
 220 |     |                     tickUpper.liquidityDelta -= int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 221 |     |                 }
 222 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityAbsoluteUnderflows(tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute, cache.liquidityBurned, 'TSL-2');
 223 |     |                 tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 224 |     |                 ticks[upper].limit = tickUpper;
 225 |     |                 clear(ticks, constants, tickMap, upper);
 226 |     |             }
 227 |     |         }
 228 |     |     }
 229 |     | 
 230 |     |      function unlock(
 231 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 232 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool,
 233 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 234 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 235 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 236 |     |     ) internal returns (
 237 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory,
 238 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory
 239 |     |     )
 240 |     |     {
 241 |     |         if (pool.liquidity > 0) return (cache, pool);
 242 |     | 
 243 |     |         (int24 startTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants, pool.price);
 244 |     | 
 245 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 246 |     |             pool.tickAtPrice = TickMap.next(tickMap, startTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, true);
 247 |     |             if (pool.tickAtPrice < ConstantProduct.maxTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing)) {
 248 |     |                 EpochMap.set(pool.tickAtPrice, zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
 249 |     |             }
 250 |     |         } else {
 251 |     |             /// @dev - roundedUp true since liquidity could be equal to the current pool tickAtPrice
 252 |     |             pool.tickAtPrice = TickMap.previous(tickMap, startTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, true);
 253 |     |             if (pool.tickAtPrice > ConstantProduct.minTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing)) {
 254 |     |                 EpochMap.set(pool.tickAtPrice, zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
 255 |     |             }
 256 |     |         }
 257 |     | 
 258 |     |         // increment pool liquidity
 259 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertPositiveLiquidityOnUnlock(ticks[pool.tickAtPrice].limit.liquidityDelta);
 260 |     |         pool.liquidity += uint128(ticks[pool.tickAtPrice].limit.liquidityDelta);
 261 |     |         int24 tickToClear = pool.tickAtPrice;
 262 |     |         uint160 tickPriceAt = ticks[pool.tickAtPrice].limit.priceAt;
 263 |     | 
 264 |     |         if (tickPriceAt == 0) {
 265 |     |             // if full tick crossed
 266 |     |             pool.price = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants);
 267 |     |         } else {
 268 |     |             // if half tick crossed
 269 |     |             pool.price = tickPriceAt;
 270 |     |             pool.tickAtPrice = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(tickPriceAt, cache.constants);
 271 |     |         }
 272 |     | 
 273 |     |         // zero out tick
 274 |     |         ticks[tickToClear].limit = PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick(0,0,0);
 275 |     |         clear(ticks, cache.constants, tickMap, tickToClear);
 276 |     | 
 277 |     |         return (cache, pool);
 278 |     |     }
 279 |     | 
 280 |     |     function clear(
 281 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 282 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
 283 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 284 |     |         int24 tickToClear
 285 |     |     ) internal {
 286 |     |         if (_empty(ticks[tickToClear])) {
 287 |     |             if (tickToClear != ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing) &&
 288 |     |                 tickToClear != ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing)) {
 289 |     |                 ticks[tickToClear].limit = PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick(0,0,0);
 290 |     |                 TickMap.unset(tickMap, tickToClear, constants.tickSpacing);
 291 |     |             }
 292 |     |         }
 293 |     |     }
 294 |     | 
 295 |     |     function _empty(
 296 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.Tick memory tick
 297 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 298 |     |         bool
 299 |     |     ) {
 300 |     |         if (tick.limit.liquidityAbsolute != 0) {
 301 |     |             return false;
 302 |     |         }
 303 |     |         return true;
 304 |     |     }
 305 |     | }

  24 |     |     function perform(
  25 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
  26 |     |             storage positions,
  27 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  28 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  29 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  30 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
  31 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
  32 |     |     ) internal {
  33 |     |         // check for invalid receiver
  34 |     |         if (params.to == address(0))
  35 |     |             require(false, 'CollectToZeroAddress()');
  36 |     | 
  37 |     |         // initialize cache
  38 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  39 |     |         cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |         // check positionId owner
  42 |     |         if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  43 |     |             require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  44 |     |         
  45 |     |         // update position
  46 |     |         (
  47 |     |             params,
  48 |     |             cache
  49 |     |         ) = LimitPositions.update(
  50 |     |             ticks,
  51 |     |             tickMap,
  52 |     |             cache,
  53 |     |             params
  54 |     |         );
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |         // save position before transfer
  57 |     |         if ((params.zeroForOne ? params.claim != cache.position.upper
  58 |     |                                : params.claim != cache.position.lower)) {
  59 |     |             if (cache.position.liquidity > 0) {
  60 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  61 |     |                     cache.position.lower = params.claim;
  62 |     |                 } else {
  63 |     |                     cache.position.upper = params.claim;
  64 |     |                 }
  65 |     |                 positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
  66 |     |             } else {
  67 |     |                 IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
  68 |     |                 delete positions[params.positionId];
  69 |     |             }
  70 |     |         } else {
  71 |     |             IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
  72 |     |             delete positions[params.positionId];
  73 |     |         }
  74 |     | 
  75 |     |         // save state before transfer call
  76 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
  77 |     |         
  78 |     |         cache = Collect.burnLimit(
  79 |     |             cache,
  80 |     |             params
  81 |     |         );
  82 |     |     }
  83 |     | 
  84 |     |     function save(
  85 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
  86 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  87 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  88 |     |     ) internal {
  89 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
  90 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
  91 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
  92 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
  93 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
  94 |     |         } else {
  95 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
  96 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
  97 |     |         }
  98 |     |     }
  99 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/limit/pool/MintLimitCall.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../LimitPositions.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../utils/Collect.sol';
   7 |     | import '../../utils/PositionTokens.sol';
   8 |     | 
   9 |     | library MintLimitCall {
  10 |     |     event MintLimit(
  11 |     |         address indexed to,
  12 |     |         int24 lower,
  13 |     |         int24 upper,
  14 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  15 |     |         uint32 positionId,
  16 |     |         uint32 epochLast,
  17 |     |         uint128 amountIn,
  18 |     |         uint128 amountFilled,
  19 |     |         uint128 liquidityMinted
  20 |     |     );
  21 |     | 
  22 |     |     event SyncLimitPool(
  23 |     |         uint160 price,
  24 |     |         uint128 liquidity,
  25 |     |         uint32 epoch,
  26 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice,
  27 |     |         bool isPool0
  28 |     |     );
  29 |     | 
  30 |     |     function perform(
  31 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
  32 |     |             storage positions,
  33 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  34 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  35 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  36 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  37 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  38 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
  39 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
  40 |     |     ) internal {
  41 |     |         if (params.positionId > 0) {
  42 |     |             if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  43 |     |                 // check for balance held
  44 |     |                 require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  45 |     |             cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  46 |     |         }
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  49 |     | 
  50 |     |         // resize position if necessary
  51 |     |         (params, cache) = LimitPositions.resize(
  52 |     |             ticks,
  53 |     |             samples,
  54 |     |             rangeTickMap,
  55 |     |             limitTickMap,
  56 |     |             params,
  57 |     |             cache
  58 |     |         );
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         if (params.positionId == 0 ||                       // new position
  61 |     |                 params.lower != cache.position.lower ||     // lower mismatch
  62 |     |                 params.upper != cache.position.upper) {     // upper mismatch
  63 |     |             LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition memory newPosition;
  64 |     |             newPosition.lower = params.lower;
  65 |     |             newPosition.upper = params.upper;
  66 |     |             // use new position in cache
  67 |     |             cache.position = newPosition;
  68 |     |             params.positionId = cache.state.positionIdNext;
  69 |     |             cache.state.positionIdNext += 1;
  70 |     |         }
  71 |     | 
  72 |     |         // save state for reentrancy safety
  73 |     |         save(cache, globalState, !params.zeroForOne);
  74 |     | 
  75 |     |         // transfer in token amount
  76 |     |         SafeTransfers.transferIn(
  77 |     |                                  params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token0 
  78 |     |                                                    : cache.constants.token1,
  79 |     |                                  params.amount + cache.swapCache.input
  80 |     |                                 );
  81 |     |         // transfer out if swap output 
  82 |     |         if (cache.swapCache.output > 0)
  83 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(
  84 |     |                 params.to,
  85 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token1 
  86 |     |                                   : cache.constants.token0,
  87 |     |                 cache.swapCache.output
  88 |     |             );
  89 |     |         // mint position if amount is left
  90 |     |         if (params.amount > 0 && params.lower < params.upper) {
  91 |     |             cache.pool = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1;
  92 |     |             // bump to the next tick if there is no liquidity
  93 |     |             if (cache.pool.liquidity == 0) {
  94 |     |                 /// @dev - this makes sure to have liquidity unlocked if undercutting
  95 |     |                 (cache, cache.pool) = LimitTicks.unlock(cache, cache.pool, ticks, limitTickMap, params.zeroForOne);
  96 |     |             }
  97 |     | 
  98 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
  99 |     |                 uint160 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 100 |     |                 if (priceLower <= cache.pool.price) {
 101 |     |                     // save liquidity if active
 102 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 103 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 104 |     |                     }
 105 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceLower;
 106 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.lower;
 107 |     |                     /// @auditor - double check liquidity is set correctly for this in insertSingle
 108 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 109 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 110 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 111 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 112 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 113 |     |                 }
 114 |     |             } else {
 115 |     |                 uint160 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 116 |     |                 if (priceUpper >= cache.pool.price) {
 117 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 118 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 119 |     |                     }
 120 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceUpper;
 121 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.upper;
 122 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 123 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 124 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 125 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 126 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 127 |     |                 }
 128 |     |             }
 129 |     |             (cache.pool, cache.position) = LimitPositions.add(
 130 |     |                 cache,
 131 |     |                 ticks,
 132 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 133 |     |                 params
 134 |     |             );
 135 |     | 
 136 |     |             // save position to storage
 137 |     |             positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
 138 |     | 
 139 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool : cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 140 |     | 
 141 |     |             emit MintLimit(
 142 |     |                 params.to,
 143 |     |                 params.lower,
 144 |     |                 params.upper,
 145 |     |                 params.zeroForOne,
 146 |     |                 params.positionId,
 147 |     |                 cache.position.epochLast,
 148 |     |                 uint128(params.amount + cache.swapCache.input),
 149 |     |                 uint128(cache.swapCache.output),
 150 |     |                 uint128(cache.liquidityMinted)
 151 |     |             );
 152 |     |         }
 153 |     | 
 154 |     |         // save lp side for safe reentrancy
 155 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
 156 |     |     }
 157 |     | 
 158 |     |     function save(
 159 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 160 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
 161 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 162 |     |     ) internal {
 163 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
 164 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
 165 |     |         globalState.positionIdNext = cache.state.positionIdNext;
 166 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 167 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 168 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
 169 |     |         } else {
 170 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 171 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
 172 |     |         }
 173 |     |     }
 174 |     | }

  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT

  8 |     | library SnapshotLimitCall {

 10 |     | 
 11 |     |     event BurnLimit(
 12 |     |         address indexed to,
 13 |     |         uint32 positionId,
 14 |     |         int24 lower,
 15 |     |         int24 upper,
 16 |     |         int24 oldClaim,
 17 |     |         int24 newClaim,
 18 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 19 |     |         uint128 liquidityBurned,
 20 |     |         uint128 tokenInClaimed,
 21 |     |         uint128 tokenOutBurned
 22 |     |     );
 23 |     | 
 24 |     |     function perform(
 25 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
 26 |     |             storage positions,
 27 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 28 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 29 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 30 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants,
 31 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.SnapshotLimitParams memory params
 32 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 33 |     |         uint128,
 34 |     |         uint128
 35 |     |     )
 36 |     |     {

 41 |     |         cache.constants = constants;

 46 |     |             positionId: params.positionId,
 47 |     |             claim: params.claim,
 48 |     |             zeroForOne: params.zeroForOne
 49 |     |         });
 50 |     |         if (cache.position.epochLast == 0) require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
 51 |     |         return LimitPositions.snapshot(
 52 |     |             ticks,
 53 |     |             tickMap,
 54 |     |             cache,
 55 |     |             burnParams
 56 |     |         );
 57 |     |     }
