/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/test/echidna/EchidnaMintLimitCall.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../libraries/limit/LimitPositions.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../libraries/utils/Collect.sol';
   7 |     | import '../../libraries/utils/PositionTokens.sol';
   8 |     | import './EchidnaAssertions.sol';
   9 |     | import '../../interfaces/IERC20Minimal.sol';
  10 |     | 
  11 | *   | library EchidnaMintLimitCall {
  12 |     | 
  13 |     |     error SimulateMint(int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionCreated);
  14 |     | 
  15 |     |     event MintLimit(
  16 |     |         address indexed to,
  17 |     |         int24 lower,
  18 |     |         int24 upper,
  19 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  20 |     |         uint32 positionId,
  21 |     |         uint32 epochLast,
  22 |     |         uint128 amountIn,
  23 |     |         uint128 amountFilled,
  24 |     |         uint128 liquidityMinted
  25 |     |     );
  26 |     | 
  27 |     |     event SyncLimitPool(
  28 |     |         uint160 price,
  29 |     |         uint128 liquidity,
  30 |     |         uint32 epoch,
  31 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice,
  32 |     |         bool isPool0
  33 |     |     );
  34 |     | 
  35 |     |     function perform(
  36 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
  37 |     |             storage positions,
  38 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  39 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  40 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  41 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  42 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  43 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
  44 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
  45 |     |     ) internal {
  46 |     |         if (params.positionId > 0) {
  47 |     |             if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  48 |     |                 // check for balance held
  49 |     |                 require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  50 |     |             cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  51 |     |         }
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  54 |     | 
  55 |     |         // resize position if necessary
  56 |     |         (params, cache) = LimitPositions.resize(
  57 |     |             ticks,
  58 |     |             samples,
  59 |     |             rangeTickMap,
  60 |     |             limitTickMap,
  61 |     |             params,
  62 |     |             cache
  63 |     |         );
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |         if (params.positionId == 0 ||                       // new position
  66 |     |                 params.lower != cache.position.lower ||     // lower mismatch
  67 |     |                 params.upper != cache.position.upper) {     // upper mismatch
  68 |     |             LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition memory newPosition;
  69 |     |             newPosition.lower = params.lower;
  70 |     |             newPosition.upper = params.upper;
  71 |     |             // use new position in cache
  72 |     |             cache.position = newPosition;
  73 |     |             params.positionId = cache.state.positionIdNext;
  74 |     |             cache.state.positionIdNext += 1;
  75 |     |         }
  76 |     | 
  77 |     |         // save state for reentrancy safety
  78 |     |         save(cache, globalState, !params.zeroForOne);
  79 |     | 
  80 |     |         // transfer in token amount
  81 |     |         SafeTransfers.transferIn(
  82 |     |                                  params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token0 
  83 |     |                                                    : cache.constants.token1,
  84 |     |                                  params.amount + cache.swapCache.input
  85 |     |                                 );
  86 |     |         // transfer out if swap output 
  87 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceeded(
  88 |     |             (params.zeroForOne ? balance(cache.constants.token1) : balance(cache.constants.token0)),
  89 |     |             cache.swapCache.output
  90 |     |         );
  91 |     |         if (cache.swapCache.output > 0)
  92 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(
  93 |     |                 params.to,
  94 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token1 
  95 |     |                                   : cache.constants.token0,
  96 |     |                 cache.swapCache.output
  97 |     |             );
  98 |     |         // mint position if amount is left
  99 |     |         if (params.amount > 0 && params.lower < params.upper) {
 100 |     |             cache.pool = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1;
 101 |     |             // bump to the next tick if there is no liquidity
 102 |     |             if (cache.pool.liquidity == 0) {
 103 |     |                 /// @dev - this makes sure to have liquidity unlocked if undercutting
 104 |     |                 (cache, cache.pool) = LimitTicks.unlock(cache, cache.pool, ticks, limitTickMap, params.zeroForOne);
 105 |     |             }
 106 |     | 
 107 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 108 |     |                 uint160 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 109 |     |                 if (priceLower <= cache.pool.price) {
 110 |     |                     // save liquidity if active
 111 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 112 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 113 |     |                     }
 114 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceLower;
 115 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.lower;
 116 |     |                     /// @auditor - double check liquidity is set correctly for this in insertSingle
 117 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 118 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 119 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 120 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 121 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 122 |     |                 }
 123 |     |             } else {
 124 |     |                 uint160 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 125 |     |                 if (priceUpper >= cache.pool.price) {
 126 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 127 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 128 |     |                     }
 129 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceUpper;
 130 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.upper;
 131 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 132 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 133 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 134 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 135 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 136 |     |                 }
 137 |     |             }
 138 |     |             (cache.pool, cache.position) = LimitPositions.add(
 139 |     |                 cache,
 140 |     |                 ticks,
 141 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 142 |     |                 params
 143 |     |             );
 144 |     | 
 145 |     |             // save position to storage
 146 |     |             positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
 147 |     | 
 148 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool 
 149 |     |                               : cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 150 |     | 
 151 |     |             emit MintLimit(
 152 |     |                 params.to,
 153 |     |                 params.lower,
 154 |     |                 params.upper,
 155 |     |                 params.zeroForOne,
 156 |     |                 params.positionId,
 157 |     |                 cache.position.epochLast,
 158 |     |                 uint128(params.amount + cache.swapCache.input),
 159 |     |                 uint128(cache.swapCache.output),
 160 |     |                 uint128(cache.liquidityMinted)
 161 |     |             );
 162 |     |         }
 163 |     |         require(cache.position.liquidity != 0, "Minting with 0 liquidity");
 164 |     |         // save lp side for safe reentrancy
 165 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
 166 |     |     }
 167 |     | 
 168 |     |     function save(
 169 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 170 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
 171 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 172 |     |     ) internal {
 173 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
 174 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
 175 |     |         globalState.positionIdNext = cache.state.positionIdNext;
 176 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 177 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 178 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
 179 |     |         } else {
 180 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 181 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
 182 |     |         }
 183 |     |     }
 184 |     | 
 185 |     |     function balance(
 186 |     |         address token
 187 |     |     ) private view returns (uint256) {
 188 |     |         (
 189 |     |             bool success,
 190 |     |             bytes memory data
 191 |     |         ) = token.staticcall(
 192 |     |                                     abi.encodeWithSelector(
 193 |     |                                         IERC20Minimal.balanceOf.selector,
 194 |     |                                         address(this)
 195 |     |                                     )
 196 |     |                                 );
 197 |     |         require(success && data.length >= 32);
 198 |     |         return abi.decode(data, (uint256));
 199 |     |     }
 200 |     | 
 201 |     |         // Echidna funcs
 202 | *   |     function getResizedTicks(
 203 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
 204 |     |             storage positions,
 205 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 206 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,

 210 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
 211 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
 212 |     |     ) external {
 213 | *   |         bool positionCreated = false;
 214 | *   |         if (params.positionId > 0) {
 215 |     |             if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
 216 |     |                 // check for balance held

 227 |     |             rangeTickMap,
 228 |     |             limitTickMap,
 229 |     |             params,
 230 |     |             cache
 231 |     |         );
 232 |     | 
 233 |     |         if (params.positionId == 0 ||                       // new position

 242 |     |             cache.state.positionIdNext += 1;
 243 |     |         }
 244 |     | 
 245 |     |         // save state for reentrancy safety
 246 |     |         save(cache, globalState, !params.zeroForOne);
 247 |     | 
 248 |     |         // transfer in token amount
 249 |     |         SafeTransfers.transferIn(
 250 |     |                                  params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token0 
 251 |     |                                                    : cache.constants.token1,
 252 |     |                                  params.amount + cache.swapCache.input
 253 |     |                                 );
 254 |     |         // transfer out if swap output 
 255 |     |         if (cache.swapCache.output > 0)
 256 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(
 257 |     |                 params.to,
 258 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token1 
 259 |     |                                   : cache.constants.token0,
 260 |     |                 cache.swapCache.output
 261 |     |             );
 262 |     |         // mint position if amount is left
 263 |     |         if (params.amount > 0 && params.lower < params.upper) {
 264 |     |             cache.pool = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1;
 265 |     |             
 266 |     |             // bump to the next tick if there is no liquidity
 267 |     |             if (cache.pool.liquidity == 0) {
 268 |     |                 /// @dev - this makes sure to have liquidity unlocked if undercutting
 269 |     |                 (cache, cache.pool) = LimitTicks.unlock(cache, cache.pool, ticks, limitTickMap, params.zeroForOne);
 270 |     |             }
 271 |     | 
 272 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 273 |     |                 uint160 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 274 |     |                 if (priceLower <= cache.pool.price) {
 275 |     |                     // save liquidity if active
 276 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 277 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 278 |     |                     }
 279 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceLower;
 280 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.lower;
 281 |     |                     /// @auditor - double check liquidity is set correctly for this in insertSingle
 282 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 283 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 284 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 285 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 286 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 287 |     |                 }
 288 |     |             } else {
 289 |     |                 uint160 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 290 |     |                 if (priceUpper >= cache.pool.price) {
 291 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 292 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 293 |     |                     }
 294 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceUpper;
 295 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.upper;
 296 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 297 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 298 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 299 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 300 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 301 |     |                 }
 302 |     |             }
 303 |     |             (cache.pool, cache.position) = LimitPositions.add(
 304 |     |                 cache,
 305 |     |                 ticks,
 306 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 307 |     |                 params
 308 |     |             );
 309 |     | 
 310 |     |             positionCreated = true;
 311 |     | 
 312 |     |             // save position to storage
 313 |     |             positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
 314 |     | 
 315 |     |             // update cache
 316 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool 
 317 |     |                               : cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 318 |     | 
 319 |     |             emit MintLimit(
 320 |     |                 params.to,
 321 |     |                 params.lower,
 322 |     |                 params.upper,
 323 |     |                 params.zeroForOne,
 324 |     |                 params.positionId,
 325 |     |                 cache.position.epochLast,
 326 |     |                 uint128(params.amount + cache.swapCache.input),
 327 |     |                 uint128(cache.swapCache.output),
 328 |     |                 uint128(cache.liquidityMinted)
 329 |     |             );
 330 |     |         }
 331 |     | 
 332 |     |         // save lp side for safe reentrancy
 333 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
 334 |     |     
 335 |     |         revert SimulateMint(params.lower, params.upper, positionCreated);
 336 |     |     }
 337 |     | }
 338 |     |

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/utils/LimitPoolManager.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../interfaces/IPool.sol';
   5 |     | import '../interfaces/limit/ILimitPool.sol';
   6 |     | import '../interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolFactory.sol';
   7 |     | import '../interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolManager.sol';
   8 |     | import '../base/events/LimitPoolManagerEvents.sol';
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | /**
  11 |     |  * @dev Defines the actions which can be executed by the factory admin.
  12 |     |  */
  13 |     | contract LimitPoolManager is ILimitPoolManager, LimitPoolManagerEvents {
  14 |     |     address public owner;
  15 |     |     address public feeTo;
  16 |     |     address public factory;
  17 |     |     uint16  public constant MAX_PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE = 1e4; /// @dev - max protocol swap fee of 100%
  18 |     |     uint16  public constant MAX_PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE = 1e2; /// @dev - max protocol fill fee of 1%
  19 |     |     // impl name => impl address
  20 |     |     mapping(bytes32 => address) internal _poolImpls;
  21 |     |     mapping(bytes32 => address) internal _tokenImpls;
  22 |     |     // swap fee => tick spacing
  23 |     |     mapping(uint16 => int16) internal _feeTiers;
  24 |     | 
  25 |     |     error InvalidSwapFee();
  26 |     |     error InvalidTickSpacing();
  27 |     |     error InvalidImplAddress();
  28 |     |     error TickSpacingAlreadyEnabled();
  29 |     |     error ImplementationAlreadyExists();
  30 |     | 
  31 |     |     constructor() {
  32 |     |         owner = msg.sender;
  33 |     |         feeTo = msg.sender;
  34 |     |         emit OwnerTransfer(address(0), msg.sender);
  35 |     | 
  36 |     |         // create initial fee tiers
  37 |     |         _feeTiers[500] = 10;
  38 |     |         _feeTiers[10000] = 100;
  39 |     |         emit FeeTierEnabled(500, 10);
  40 |     |         emit FeeTierEnabled(10000, 100);
  41 |     |     }
  42 |     | 
  43 |     |     /**
  44 |     |      * @dev Throws if called by any account other than the owner.
  45 |     |      */
  46 |     |     modifier onlyOwner() {
  47 |     |         _checkOwner();
  48 |     |         _;
  49 |     |     }
  50 |     | 
  51 |     |     modifier onlyFeeTo() {
  52 |     |         _checkFeeTo();
  53 |     |         _;
  54 |     |     }
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |     /**
  57 |     |      * @dev Transfers ownership of the contract to a new account (`newOwner`).
  58 |     |      * Can only be called by the current owner.
  59 |     |      */
  60 |     |     function transferOwner(address newOwner) public virtual onlyOwner {
  61 |     |         if(newOwner == address(0)) require (false, 'TransferredToZeroAddress()');
  62 |     |         _transferOwner(newOwner);
  63 |     |     }
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |     function transferFeeTo(address newFeeTo) public virtual onlyFeeTo {
  66 |     |         if(newFeeTo == address(0)) require (false, 'TransferredToZeroAddress()');
  67 |     |         _transferFeeTo(newFeeTo);
  68 |     |     }
  69 |     | 
  70 |     |     /**
  71 |     |      * @dev Transfers ownership of the contract to a new account (`newOwner`).
  72 |     |      * Internal function without access restriction.
  73 |     |      */
  74 |     |     function _transferOwner(address newOwner) internal virtual {
  75 |     |         address oldOwner = owner;
  76 |     |         owner = newOwner;
  77 |     |         emit OwnerTransfer(oldOwner, newOwner);
  78 |     |     }
  79 |     | 
  80 |     |     /**
  81 |     |      * @dev Transfers fee collection to a new account (`newFeeTo`).
  82 |     |      * Internal function without access restriction.
  83 |     |      */
  84 |     |     function _transferFeeTo(address newFeeTo) internal virtual {
  85 |     |         address oldFeeTo = feeTo;
  86 |     |         feeTo = newFeeTo;
  87 |     |         emit OwnerTransfer(oldFeeTo, newFeeTo);
  88 |     |     }
  89 |     | 
  90 |     |     function enableTickSpacing(
  91 |     |         int16 tickSpacing,
  92 |     |         uint16 swapFee
  93 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
  94 |     |         if (_feeTiers[swapFee] != 0) revert TickSpacingAlreadyEnabled();
  95 |     |         if (tickSpacing <= 0) revert InvalidTickSpacing();
  96 |     |         if (tickSpacing % 2 != 0) revert InvalidTickSpacing();
  97 |     |         if (swapFee == 0) revert InvalidSwapFee();
  98 |     |         if (swapFee > 10000) revert InvalidSwapFee();
  99 |     |         _feeTiers[swapFee] = tickSpacing;
 100 |     |         emit FeeTierEnabled(swapFee, tickSpacing);
 101 |     |     }
 102 |     | 
 103 |     |     function enableImplementation(
 104 |     |         bytes32 poolType_,
 105 |     |         address poolImpl_,
 106 |     |         address tokenImpl_
 107 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
 108 |     |         if (_poolImpls[poolType_] != address(0)) revert ImplementationAlreadyExists();
 109 |     |         if (poolImpl_ == address(0) || tokenImpl_ == address(0)) revert InvalidImplAddress();
 110 |     |         /// @dev - prevent same addresses since factory does not support this
 111 |     |         if (poolImpl_ == tokenImpl_) revert InvalidImplAddress();
 112 |     |         _poolImpls[poolType_] = poolImpl_;
 113 |     |         _tokenImpls[poolType_] = tokenImpl_;
 114 |     |         emit ImplementationEnabled(poolType_, poolImpl_, tokenImpl_);
 115 |     |     }
 116 |     | 
 117 |     |     function setFactory(
 118 |     |         address factory_
 119 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
 120 |     |         if (factory != address(0)) require (false, 'FactoryAlreadySet()');
 121 |     |         emit FactoryChanged(factory, factory_);
 122 |     |         factory = factory_;
 123 |     |     }
 124 |     | 
 125 |     |     function collectProtocolFees(
 126 |     |         address[] calldata pools
 127 |     |     ) external {
 128 |     |         if (pools.length == 0) require (false, 'EmptyPoolsArray()');
 129 |     |         uint128[] memory token0FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 130 |     |         uint128[] memory token1FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 131 |     |         // pass empty fees params
 132 |     |         FeesParams memory feesParams;
 133 |     |         for (uint i; i < pools.length;) {
 134 |     |             (
 135 |     |                 token0FeesCollected[i],
 136 |     |                 token1FeesCollected[i]
 137 |     |             ) = IPool(pools[i]).fees(feesParams);
 138 |     |             unchecked {
 139 |     |                 ++i;
 140 |     |             }
 141 |     |         }
 142 |     |         emit ProtocolFeesCollected(pools, token0FeesCollected, token1FeesCollected);
 143 |     |     }
 144 |     | 
 145 |     |     // protocol fee flags
 146 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_0 = 2**0;
 147 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_1 = 2**1;
 148 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_0 = 2**2;
 149 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_1 = 2**3;
 150 |     | 
 151 |     |     function modifyProtocolFees(
 152 |     |         address[] calldata pools,
 153 |     |         FeesParams[] calldata feesParams
 154 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
 155 |     |         if (pools.length == 0) require (false, 'EmptyPoolsArray()');
 156 |     |         if (pools.length != feesParams.length) {
 157 |     |             require (false, 'MismatchedArrayLengths()');
 158 |     |         }
 159 |     |         uint128[] memory token0FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 160 |     |         uint128[] memory token1FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 161 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolSwapFees0 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 162 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolSwapFees1 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 163 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolFillFees0 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 164 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolFillFees1 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 165 |     |         for (uint i; i < pools.length;) {
 166 |     |             (
 167 |     |                 token0FeesCollected[i],
 168 |     |                 token1FeesCollected[i]
 169 |     |             ) = IPool(pools[i]).fees(
 170 |     |                 feesParams[i]
 171 |     |             );
 172 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_0) > 0) {
 173 |     |                 protocolSwapFees0[i] = feesParams[i].protocolSwapFee0;
 174 |     |             }
 175 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_1) > 0) {
 176 |     |                 protocolSwapFees1[i] = feesParams[i].protocolSwapFee1;
 177 |     |             }
 178 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_0) > 0) {
 179 |     |                 protocolFillFees0[i] = feesParams[i].protocolFillFee0;
 180 |     |             }
 181 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_1) > 0) {
 182 |     |                 protocolFillFees1[i] = feesParams[i].protocolFillFee1;
 183 |     |             }
 184 |     |             // else values will remain zero
 185 |     |             unchecked {
 186 |     |                 ++i;
 187 |     |             }
 188 |     |         }
 189 |     |         emit ProtocolSwapFeesModified(
 190 |     |             pools,
 191 |     |             protocolSwapFees0,
 192 |     |             protocolSwapFees1
 193 |     |         );
 194 |     |         emit ProtocolFillFeesModified(
 195 |     |             pools,
 196 |     |             protocolFillFees0,
 197 |     |             protocolFillFees1
 198 |     |         );
 199 |     |         emit ProtocolFeesCollected(
 200 |     |             pools,
 201 |     |             token0FeesCollected,
 202 |     |             token1FeesCollected
 203 |     |         );
 204 |     |     }
 205 |     | 
 206 |     |     function implementations(
 207 |     |         bytes32 key
 208 |     |     ) external view returns (
 209 |     |         address,
 210 |     |         address
 211 |     |     ) {
 212 |     |         return (_poolImpls[key], _tokenImpls[key]);
 213 |     |     }
 214 |     | 
 215 |     |     function feeTiers(
 216 |     |         uint16 swapFee
 217 |     |     ) external view returns (
 218 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 219 |     |     ) {
 220 |     |         return _feeTiers[swapFee];
 221 |     |     }
 222 |     |     
 223 |     |     /**
 224 |     |      * @dev Throws if the sender is not the owner.
 225 |     |      */
 226 |     |     function _checkOwner() internal view {
 227 |     |         if (owner != msg.sender) require (false, 'OwnerOnly()');
 228 |     |     }
 229 |     | 
 230 |     |     /**
 231 |     |      * @dev Throws if the sender is not the feeTo.
 232 |     |      */
 233 |     |     function _checkFeeTo() internal view {
 234 |     |         if (feeTo != msg.sender) require (false, 'FeeToOnly()');
 235 |     |     }
 236 |     | }

  18 |     |

  25 |     |

  28 |     | 
  29 |     |     constructor(
  30 |     |         address factory_
  31 |     |     ) {
  32 |     |         factory = factory_;
  33 |     |         original = address(this);
  34 |     |     }
  35 |     | 
  36 |     |     /// @dev token id => owner => balance
  37 |     |     mapping(uint256 => mapping(address => uint256)) private _tokenBalances;
  38 |     |

  41 |     |

  43 |     |     mapping(uint256 => uint256) private _totalSupplyById;
  44 |     | 
  45 |     |     string private constant _NAME = "Poolshark LP";
  46 |     |     string private constant _SYMBOL = "PSHARK-LP";
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |     modifier onlyCanonicalClones(
  49 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
  50 |     |     ) {
  51 |     |         if(!_onlyCanonicalPools(constants)) require (false, 'CanoncialPoolsOnly()');
  52 |     |         if(!_onlyCanonicalPoolTokens(constants)) require (false, 'CanoncialPoolTokensOnly()');
  53 |     |         _;
  54 |     |     }
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |     modifier checkApproval(address _from, address _spender) {
  57 |     |         if (_from != _spender)
  58 |     |             if(!_isApprovedForAll(_from, _spender)) 
  59 |     |                 revert SpenderNotApproved(_from, _spender);
  60 |     |         _;
  61 |     |     }
  62 |     | 
  63 |     |     modifier checkAddresses(address _from, address _to) {
  64 |     |         if (_from == address(0) || _to == address(0)) revert TransferFromOrToAddress0();
  65 |     |         if (_from == _to) revert TransferToSelf();
  66 |     |         _;
  67 |     |     }
  68 |     | 
  69 |     |     modifier checkLength(uint256 _lengthA, uint256 _lengthB) {
  70 |     |         if (_lengthA != _lengthB) revert LengthMismatch(_lengthA, _lengthB);
  71 |     |         _;
  72 |     |     }
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |     modifier checkERC1155Support(address recipient) {
  75 |     |         if (!_verifyERC1155Support(recipient)) revert ERC1155NotSupported();
  76 |     |         _;
  77 |     |     }
  78 |     |

  84 |     |     ) external 
  85 |     |         onlyCanonicalClones(constants)
  86 |     |         checkERC1155Support(_account)

  89 |     |     }

  96 |     |     ) external
  97 |     |         onlyCanonicalClones(constants)
  98 |     |     {
  99 |     |         _burn(_account, _id, _amount);
 100 |     |     }
 101 |     | 
 102 |     |     function setApprovalForAll(address _spender, bool _approved) public virtual override {
 103 |     |         _setApprovalForAll(msg.sender, _spender, _approved);
 104 |     |     }
 105 |     | 
 106 |     |     function safeTransferFrom(
 107 |     |         address _from,
 108 |     |         address _to,
 109 |     |         uint256 _id,
 110 |     |         uint256 _amount
 111 |     |     ) public virtual override
 112 |     |         checkAddresses(_from, _to)
 113 |     |         checkApproval(_from, msg.sender)
 114 |     |         checkERC1155Support(_to)
 115 |     |     {
 116 |     |         address _spender = msg.sender;
 117 |     |         _transfer(_from, _to, _id, _amount);
 118 |     |         emit TransferSingle(_spender, _from, _to, _id, _amount);
 119 |     |     }
 120 |     | 
 121 |     |     function safeBatchTransferFrom(
 122 |     |         address _from,
 123 |     |         address _to,
 124 |     |         uint256[] calldata _ids,
 125 |     |         uint256[] calldata _amounts
 126 |     |     ) public virtual override
 127 |     |         checkLength(_ids.length, _amounts.length)
 128 |     |         checkAddresses(_from, _to)
 129 |     |         checkApproval(_from, msg.sender)
 130 |     |         checkERC1155Support(_to)
 131 |     |     {
 132 |     |         unchecked {
 133 |     |             for (uint256 i; i < _ids.length; ++i) {
 134 |     |                 _transfer(_from, _to, _ids[i], _amounts[i]);
 135 |     |             }
 136 |     |         }
 137 |     |         emit TransferBatch(msg.sender, _from, _to, _ids, _amounts);
 138 |     |     }

 140 |     |     function isApprovedForAll(address _owner, address _spender) public view virtual override returns (bool) {
 141 |     |         return _isApprovedForAll(_owner, _spender);
 142 |     |     }

 145 |     |       return  interfaceID == 0x01ffc9a7 ||    // ERC-165 support
 146 |     |               interfaceID == 0xd9b67a26;      // ERC-1155 support
 147 |     |     }

 159 |     |     }
 160 |     | 
 161 |     |     function balanceOf(address _account, uint256 _id) public view virtual override returns (uint256) {
 162 |     |         return _tokenBalances[_id][_account];
 163 |     |     }
 164 |     | 
 165 |     |     function balanceOfBatch(
 166 |     |         address[] calldata _accounts,
 167 |     |         uint256[] calldata _ids
 168 |     |     ) public view virtual override
 169 |     |         checkLength(_accounts.length, _ids.length)
 170 |     |         returns (uint256[] memory batchBalances)
 171 |     |     {
 172 |     |         batchBalances = new uint256[](_accounts.length);
 173 |     |         unchecked {
 174 |     |             for (uint256 i; i < _accounts.length; ++i) {
 175 |     |                 batchBalances[i] = balanceOf(_accounts[i], _ids[i]);
 176 |     |             }
 177 |     |         }
 178 |     |     }
 179 |     | 
 180 |     |     function _mint(
 181 |     |         address _account,
 182 |     |         uint256 _id,
 183 |     |         uint256 _amount
 184 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 185 |     |         if (_account == address(0)) revert MintToAddress0();
 186 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(address(0), _account, _id, _amount);
 187 |     |         _totalSupplyById[_id] += _amount;
 188 |     |         uint256 _accountBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_account];
 189 |     |         unchecked {
 190 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_account] = _accountBalance + _amount;
 191 |     |         }
 192 |     |         emit TransferSingle(msg.sender, address(0), _account, _id, _amount);
 193 |     |     }
 194 |     | 
 195 |     |     function _burn(
 196 |     |         address _account,
 197 |     |         uint256 _id,
 198 |     |         uint256 _amount
 199 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 200 |     |         if (_account == address(0)) revert BurnFromAddress0();
 201 |     |         uint256 _accountBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_account];
 202 |     |         if (_accountBalance < _amount) revert BurnExceedsBalance(_account, _id, _amount);
 203 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(_account, address(0), _id, _amount);
 204 |     |         unchecked {
 205 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_account] = _accountBalance - _amount;
 206 |     |             _totalSupplyById[_id] -= _amount;
 207 |     |         }
 208 |     |         emit TransferSingle(msg.sender, _account, address(0), _id, _amount);
 209 |     |     }
 210 |     | 
 211 |     |     function _transfer(
 212 |     |         address _from,
 213 |     |         address _to,
 214 |     |         uint256 _id,
 215 |     |         uint256 _amount
 216 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 217 |     |         uint256 _fromBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_from];
 218 |     |         if (_fromBalance < _amount) revert TransferExceedsBalance(_from, _id, _amount);
 219 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(_from, _to, _id, _amount);
 220 |     |         unchecked {
 221 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_from] = _fromBalance - _amount;
 222 |     |         }
 223 |     |         uint256 _toBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_to];
 224 |     |         unchecked {
 225 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_to] = _toBalance + _amount;
 226 |     |         }
 227 |     |     }
 228 |     | 
 229 |     |     function _setApprovalForAll(
 230 |     |         address _owner,
 231 |     |         address _spender,
 232 |     |         bool _approved
 233 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 234 |     |         if (_owner == _spender) revert SelfApproval(_owner);
 235 |     |         _spenderApprovals[_owner][_spender] = _approved;
 236 |     |         emit ApprovalForAll(_owner, _spender, _approved);
 237 |     |     }
 238 |     | 
 239 |     |     function _isApprovedForAll(address _owner, address _spender) internal view virtual returns (bool) {
 240 |     |         return _owner == _spender || _spenderApprovals[_owner][_spender];
 241 |     |     }
 242 |     | 
 243 |     |     /// @notice Hook that is called before any token transfer.
 244 |     |     function _beforeTokenTransfer(
 245 |     |         address from,
 246 |     |         address to,
 247 |     |         uint256 id,
 248 |     |         uint256 amount
 249 |     |     ) internal virtual {}
 250 |     | 
 251 |     |     function _onlyCanonicalPoolTokens(
 252 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 253 |     |     ) private view returns (bool) {
 254 |     |         // generate key for pool
 255 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
 256 |     |             poolImpl(),
 257 |     |             constants.token0,
 258 |     |             constants.token1,
 259 |     |             constants.swapFee
 260 |     |         ));
 261 |     | 
 262 |     |         // compute address
 263 |     |         address predictedAddress = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 264 |     |             original,
 265 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 266 |     |                 poolImpl()
 267 |     |             ),
 268 |     |             key,
 269 |     |             factory
 270 |     |         );
 271 |     | 
 272 |     |         if (predictedAddress != address(this)) return false;
 273 |     | 
 274 |     |         return true;
 275 |     |     }
 276 |     | 
 277 |     |     function _onlyCanonicalPools(
 278 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.Immutables memory constants
 279 |     |     ) private view returns (bool) {
 280 |     |         // generate key for pool
 281 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
 282 |     |             poolImpl(),
 283 |     |             constants.token0,
 284 |     |             constants.token1,
 285 |     |             constants.swapFee
 286 |     |         ));
 287 |     | 
 288 |     |         // compute address
 289 |     |         address predictedAddress = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 290 |     |             poolImpl(),
 291 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 292 |     |                 constants.owner,
 293 |     |                 constants.token0,
 294 |     |                 constants.token1,
 295 |     |                 constants.poolToken,
 296 |     |                 constants.bounds.min,
 297 |     |                 constants.bounds.max,
 298 |     |                 constants.genesisTime,
 299 |     |                 constants.tickSpacing,
 300 |     |                 constants.swapFee
 301 |     |             ),
 302 |     |             key,
 303 |     |             factory
 304 |     |         );
 305 |     | 
 306 |     |         if (predictedAddress != msg.sender) return false;
 307 |     | 
 308 |     |         return true;
 309 |     |     }
 310 |     | 
 311 |     |     /// @notice Return if the `_target` contract supports ERC-1155 interface
 312 |     |     /// @param _target The address of the contract
 313 |     |     /// @return supported Whether the contract is supported (true) or not (false)
 314 |     |     function _verifyERC1155Support(address _target) private view returns (bool supported) {
 315 |     |         if (_target.code.length == 0) return true;
 316 |     |         bytes memory encodedParams = abi.encodeWithSelector(
 317 |     |             IERC165.supportsInterface.selector,
 318 |     |             type(IPositionERC1155).interfaceId
 319 |     |         );
 320 |     |         (bool success, bytes memory result) = _target.staticcall{gas: 30_000}(encodedParams);
 321 |     |         if (result.length < 32) return false;
 322 |     |         return success && abi.decode(result, (bool));
 323 |     |     }
 324 |     | }
